Chapter i kuv ish-veh had ri sov-mashau fi' wuh ac'ruth lau asal valancy stirling's bosh ha'kiv would ma vesh' entirely natya. She would ma hal-tor, k' wuh shom t' ish-veh maat, tor ezyet wellington's engagement picnic heh dr. Trent would ma hal-tor tor montreal. Tonk'peh ish-veh did sov-masu heh du dungau zhu-tor ra pavesh-tor tor ish-veh fai'ei t' ish-veh. Valancy wakened lehkuh-mal, svi' wuh lifeless, hopeless wadan aishan preceding gad-keshtan. She had ri yuk-tor maut muhl. Veh tor ri yuk muhl, sometimes, lu veh nam-tor dah-leh-naukuh fi' wuh morrow, heh unmarried, svi' wuh shila heh tersaya wilat wuh unmarried nam-tor veling eifa vi ma vravshau tor prah wuh sasu. Deerwood heh wuh stirlings had wu opi' relegated valancy tor hopeless hinek maidenhood. Tonk'peh valancy herself had worla ved relinquished wuh ac'ruth pitiful, shamed, pi' rok ik romance would sarlah ish-veh yut yetnever, abi' nash masupik, horrible asal, lu she wakened tor wuh kla-min ik she vesh' dah-leh-naukuh heh unsought k' sovek sasu. Ay, tra' ti wuh rakus. Valancy did ri kashek ni mau hasu wuh hinek maid. Po' ek', she nahp, hasu wuh hinek maid couldn't possibly nam-tor u' dreadful u' hasu telik tor wuh sa-kuk wellington il wuh sa-kuk benjamin, il kauk wuh sa-kuk herbert. Ra dash-tor ish-veh vesh' ik she had worla had wuh pavesh tor nam-tor sovek-vel tonk'peh wuh hinek maid. Rai sasu had ek'wak aitlu ish-veh. Wuh bezhun-masu sarlah vi' ish-veh bezhun u' she ti tra' sa'awek svi' wuh faintly greying mu'khlup'es. She dared ri kal-tor herself maf u' lerash u' she aitlu tor, na' dahkuh utvau. She vesh' kwes ik maf-tor lau katau fi' wuh'ashiv nashiv-tor t' ik kusut pa' wuh khaf-spol. She had had wuh spell t' ish-veh po' she had prah vi' bedrather weh-rasahkos do sovek she had had wi. Heh she vesh' kwes ish-veh ko-mekh would beglanau ish-veh yon-kur bezhun na' asal-yem heh potau na' ish-veh k' minute, persistent, mosquito-spo' deshkau fundauik wuh aishan thereof. "suppose, " nahp valancy k' wuh ghastly wa'limatau, "i kilko-tor k' wuh eiktra yeht'es, 'i am maf-tor fai'ei i fam yehat prah telik.' uf horrified ko-mekh would bethough she nam-tor kafusik kanok gad t' ish-veh ha'kiv t' ish-veh hinek maid ko-fu." tonk'peh veling appearances dang nam-tor potau abru. "ish-veh nam-tor ri, " valancy kupi zhu-tor ish-veh ko-mekh's prim, dictatorial spes asserting, "ish-veh nam-tor ri maidenly tor nah-tor pa' sasu." wuh nahp t' ish-veh ko-mekh's sagluvaya tor valancy laughfor she had wuh kash-ral t' humour kling svi' ish-veh maat suspected. Na' ik tukh, tra' vesh' wuh rom wehk vel pa' valancy ik kling suspected. Tonk'peh ish-veh laughter vesh' maut superficial heh presently she ti tra', wuh huddled, futile pi' khlop, listening tor wuh sov-masu pouring ne' s'udish heh watching, k' wuh has-bosh distaste, wuh chill, merciless ta'hal creeping vi' ish-veh watosh, sordid tvi-shal. She fai-tor wuh ugliness t' ik tvi-shal k' heartknew ish-veh heh fnu-ven ish-veh. Wuh kin-kur-kras-tor lan-tol, k' veh hideous, "hooked" la'y k' wuh sar-tak, k' wuh grotesque, "hooked" dog fi' ish-veh, kwon-hau-ov grinning na' ish-veh lu she awoke; wuh spoh-tor, gu'gelik-yon-kur dun; wuh abru-tol discoloured k' hinek tasau heh tuhsau k' treshaya; wuh wonil, k'hy pi' washstand; wuh khav-kur-dun lambrequin k' gahv-kur roses fi' ish-veh; wuh gla-tor hinek looking-makh k' wuh treshaya mes' ish-veh, propped abru fi' wuh inadequate sai-vel-tor-pasu; wuh kak t' t'kahr potpourri tor k' ish-veh ko-mekh svi' ish-veh mythical honeymoon; wuh fo-wein-tor natuhn, k' veh thorau teruk, if krei stickles had tor svi' ish-veh kaing mythical girlhood; wuh beaded pincushion k' ulef its o'lid geldel hal-tor; wuh veh stegel, kin-kur ku-san; wuh spoh-tor hinek motto, "hal-tor tonk'peh ri yen-tor, " ar'kada svi' kur-tor yarns pa' lo'uk-grand-ko-mekh stirling's grim hinek limuk; wuh hinek ha'gel-bikuv t' t'kahr tomasu wu klee'fah'tu s' wuh tvi-shal ne'. Tra' vesh' goh dahkuh bikuv ik vesh' ri t' tomasu. Veh, wuh hinek chromo t' wuh wil'tei sitting fi' wuh sov-masuyanik svep-ashef. Ik bikuv kwon-hau-ov tor valancy unhappy. Ik forlorn pi' dog crouched fi' wuh svep-ashef svi' wuh driving sov-masu! Po didn't ein veh tu'ash wuh svep heh kal-tor ish-veh svi'? Wuh vath bikuv vesh' wuh spoh-tor, passe-partouted thes t' ko-te'kru louise coming ne' wuh stairway, if ezyet wellington had lavishly putan-tor ish-veh fi' ish-veh tenth gad t'keshtan. Na' leh-nau tevun she had glazhau na' ish-veh heh fnu-ven ish-veh, vaksurik, smug, shal-satisfied ko-te'kru louise. Tonk'peh she worla dared vashau ish-veh il snem-tor ish-veh. Ko-mekh heh krei stickles would ma vesh' aghast, il, u' valancy irreverently sagluvau ish-veh svi' ish-veh nahp, would ma had wuh nunau. Kanok tvi-shal svi' wuh kelek vesh' watosh, veling. Tonk'peh downstairs appearances vesh' potau abru somewhat. Tra' vesh' rai donku na' tvi-shal kling ek'wak gla-tor. Valancy sometimes olau ik she kupi ma ovsoh vel na' ish-veh tvi-shal herself, kauk rik' donku, kuv she vesh' permitted. Tonk'peh ish-veh ko-mekh had negatived kanok timid suggestion heh valancy did ri persist. Valancy worla persisted. She vesh' kwes tor. Ish-veh ko-mekh kupi ri brook opposition. Mrs. Stirling would sulk na' gad kuv puthrap-tor, k' wuh airs t' wuh insulted duchess. Wuh goh vel valancy tishau pa' ish-veh tvi-shal vesh' ik she kupi nam-tor sa'awek tra' na' mu-yor tor maf kuv she aitlu tor. Tonk'peh, po' ek', ra did ish-veh tukh kuv wuh tvi-shal, if du nam-tor-tor na' nothing kaula sleeping heh sai-vel-tor svi', vesh' watosh? Valancy vesh' worla permitted tor stay sa'awek svi' ish-veh tvi-shal na' sovek vath lof. Sutra vi aitlu tor nam-tor sa'awek, ni mrs. Frederick stirling heh krei stickles pudva-tor, kupi goh aitlun tor nam-tor sa'awek na' ein sinister lof. Tonk'peh ish-veh tvi-shal svi' wuh pla-kur castle vesh' kanok-vei wuh tvi-shal dang nam-tor. Valancy, ni cowed heh nessau heh overridden heh snubbed svi' yeht ha'kiv, vesh' wont tor kal-tor herself hal-tor rather splendidly svi' ish-veh gad-sahr-tor-tor. Kling svi' wuh stirling maat, il its ramifications, suspected nash, least t' ek' ish-veh ko-mekh heh krei stickles. Au worla fai-tor ik valancy had dahkuh homesthe watosh yon-kur dok natuhn t' wuh ha-kel, fi' elm yut, heh wuh pla-kur castle svi' spain. Valancy had ha-tor spiritually svi' wuh pla-kur castle ek'wak opi' she kupi vokau. She had vesh' wuh maut tiny kan lu she afer-tor herself ma t' ish-veh. Kwon-hau-ov, lu she ikap-tor ish-veh bezhun, she kupi gla-tor ish-veh plainly, k' its turrets heh hai-sovek fi' wuh pine-clad suk'kunel pidek, wrapped svi' its faint, pla-kur loveliness, tehnat wuh tev-tor igen t' wuh rom heh ri-fainu solektra. Kanok-vei wonderful heh vaksurik vesh' svi' ik castle. Ek'zer ik ko-te'kru lau ma worn; pelal t' moonlight heh yon; ku-san t' roses heh pi-maat-tukh; wu hash t' gan marble ash-tor, k' lo'uk, wan-kur urns, heh k' slender, mist-clad maidens going abru heh ne' au; kelek, marble-pillared, wilat shimmering mashulek tevan-tor heh nightingales sang among wuh myrtles; tvur t' haulat ik haul-tor goh handsome knights heh lovely womenherself wuh loveliest t' ek', na' t'vi glance sasu tev-tor. Ek' ik nenikau ish-veh k'fai wuh boredom t' ish-veh gad vesh' wuh rok t' going fi' wuh sahr-tor spree na' mu-yor. Danik, kuv ri ek', t' wuh stirlings would ma tev-tor t' horror kuv au had fainu ulef wuh vel valancy did svi' ish-veh pla-kur castle. Na' veh vel she had ved wuh zamu lovers svi' ish-veh. Oh, goh veh na' wuh wak. Veh vi wooed ish-veh k' ek' wuh romantic ardour t' wuh ya'shakhuv t' chivalry heh skil-tor ish-veh po' wu vaikaya heh wehk deeds t' derring-tor, heh vesh' wedded tor ish-veh k' pomp heh circumstance svi' wuh lo'uk, hai-sovek-geldau chapel t' wuh pla-kur castle. Na' leh-dah, nash lover vesh' wuh rom lad k' pi-maat-kur tcha-tor heh heavenly pla-kur bezhun. Na' leh-kau, au vesh' ha-vol heh gu'gelik heh spoh, tonk'peh fam dvun necessarily handsome. Na' dah-leh, au vesh' ascetic, dreamy, spiritual. Na' dah-leh-kaukuh, au had wuh sok'i-tresahk ahs, slightly grim, heh wuh limuk karik heh rugged rather do handsome. Valancy worla grew older do dah-leh-kaukuh svi' ish-veh pla-kur castle, tonk'peh recentlyvery recentlyher hero had had reddish, tawny isachya, wuh kuvoran-tor abru'teruklar-ru'lut heh wuh mysterious vesht. I ri tor leralmin valancy deliberately riyeht-stau aifa lovers u' she outgrew au. Veh veling spoh-tor maf u' wuh'ashiv sarlah. Vel nam-tor maut convenient svi' nash respect svi' pla-kur castles. Tonk'peh, fi' nash asal t' ish-veh gad t' buk, valancy kupi ri talal wuh tal-muv t' ish-veh pla-kur castle. Reality hish-tor fi' ish-veh nuh' hardly, barking na' ish-veh timut spo' wuh maddening pi' dog. She vesh' dah-leh-naukuh, lonely, undesired, has-bosh-favouredthe goh homely ko-kan svi' wuh handsome maat, k' rai vesht heh rai fa-wak. U' irak u' she kupi glazhau pla', ha'kiv vesh' drab heh colourless, k' ri veh single hirat-kur il gahv-kur gla-tor sovek-wilat. U' irak u' she kupi glazhau fa'rak ish-veh seemed ac'ruth tor nam-tor aishan wuh ka abi' she vesh' nothing tonk'peh wuh solitary, pi' withered mor clinging tor wuh wintry bough. Wuh moment lu wuh kosu realises ik she has nothing tor ha-tor forneither ashaya, gu-vam, lof il hopeholds na' ish-veh wuh bitterness t' tevakh. "heh i aishan ma tor hal-tor fi' living fai'ei i mokuhlek't pehkaya. I lau ma tor ha-tor oh-leh tevun, " nahp valancy, svi' wuh ves t' pahth. "etek're ek' horribly wu-ha-tor. Ish-veh sickens me tor nah-tor t' ish-veh." she vesh' glad ish-veh vesh' rainingor rather, she vesh' drearily satisfied ik ish-veh vesh' raining. Tra' would nam-tor rai picnic ik gad. Nash kanok-tevunik picnic, whereby ezyet heh sa-kuk wellingtonone kwon-hau-ov nahp t' au svi' ik successioninevitably u'thet ish-veh engagement na' wuh picnic reh-leh tevun fa', had vesh', t' tab-ma tevun, wuh veritable yuk-eshu'a tor valancy. K' wuh impish coincidence ish-veh vesh' wuh ka gad u' ish-veh gad t'keshtan heh, po' she had be' dvun-tor dah-leh-kaukuh, kling kal-tor ish-veh yen-tor ish-veh. Mau u' she fnu-ven going tor wuh picnic, ish-veh would worla ma paresh-tor tor ish-veh tor rebel tehnat ish-veh. Tra' seemed tor nam-tor nothing t' wuh revolutionary svi' ish-veh malat. Heh she fai-tor exactly ra kanok veh would leralmin tor ish-veh na' wuh picnic. Sa-kuk wellington, ik she ritishau heh despised kauk hi au had fulfilled wuh k'lek stirling aspiration, "marrying donku, " would leralmin tor ish-veh svi' wuh pig's zhal, "ri thinking t' getting telik wi, t'nash-veh tal-kam?" heh yi hal-tor ska' vi' wuh vlei t' laughter k' if au invariably concluded ish-veh pasik remarks. Ezyet wellington, t' ik valancy lam-tor svi' abject teshan, would var-tor ish-veh pa' olive's uzh chiffon sai-vel heh cecil's kim-shah vaikau nuhm. Valancy would ma tor glazhau u' sanoi heh interested u' kuv wuh sai-vel heh nuhm had vesh' ish-veh il else ezyet wellington would nam-tor puthrap-tor. Heh valancy had wu ago klopau ik she would rather thrap-tor oekon do ezyet wellington, fai'ei oekon lau forgive ish-veh tonk'peh ezyet wellington worla would. Ezyet alberta, enormously thelik, k' wuh amiable es'merka t' kwon-hau-ov referring tor ish-veh sa-telsu u' "au, " u' kuv au vesh' wuh goh sa creature svi' wuh panu, vi kupi worla yen-tor ik she had vesh' wuh lo'uk vaksur svi' ish-veh youth, would condole k' valancy fi' ish-veh sallow wadi "i ri tor fai-tor po ek' wuh ko-kan t' nash-gad nam-tor ni sunburned. Lu i vesh' wuh ko-kan t'nash-veh wadi vesh' roses heh dyrk. I vesh' tum-tor wuh prettiest ko-kan svi' canada, t'nash-veh tal-kam." sos'eh sa-kuk herbert wouldn't leralmin anythingor sos'eh au would remark jocularly, "uf thelik du're getting, doss!" heh yi kanok-veh would abru'teruklar-ru'lut abru' wuh excessively humorous idea t' ri donku-tor, scrawny pi' doss getting thelik. Handsome, solemn sa-kuk james, ik valancy ritishau tonk'peh respected fai'ei au vesh' reputed tor nam-tor maut clever heh vesh' therefore wuh maat oraclebrains hasu rim nuh' plentiful svi' wuh stirling connectionwould probably remark k' wuh owl-spo' sarcasm ik had skil-tor ish-veh ish-veh reputation, "i suppose du're toranik k' ish-veh rok-tuf aifa gad?" heh sa-kuk benjamin would ya'akash ein t' ish-veh abominable conundrums, svi' wheezy chuckles, heh kilko-srashiv au himself. "ra nam-tor wuh natyan svi' doss heh wuh aushfa? "wuh aushfa istau tor klau wuh thuhk heh doss istau tor sem-rik wuh au's." valancy had puzhu-tor ish-veh ya'akash ik riddle kau-leh wak heh kanok wak she aitlu tor lehm vel na' ish-veh. Tonk'peh she worla did. Svi' wuh wuh'rak shi, wuh stirlings veling did ri lehm vel; svi' wuh dahr shi, sa-kuk benjamin vesh' wuh wealthy heh childless hinek kir'an heh valancy had vesh' katau abru svi' wuh pthak heh admonition t' ish-veh donku. Kuv she puthrap-tor ish-veh au would tresahk ish-veh s' ish-veh willsupposing she vesh' svi' ish-veh. Valancy did ri aitlun tor nam-tor tresahk s' sa-kuk benjamin's dungi. She had vesh' ri donku-tor ek' ish-veh ha'kiv heh fai-tor wuh galling bitterness t' ish-veh. Ni she palesh-tor ish-veh riddles heh kauk abru'teruklar-ru'lut tortured pi' abru'teruklar-ru'lut abru' au. Ezyet isabel, downright heh disagreeable u' wuh she'rak salan, would criticise ish-veh svi' ein wayvalancy kupi ri predict aishan uf, na' ezyet isabel worla ashiv-tor wuh criticismshe afer-tor vel uzh k' if tor jab du kanok wak. Ezyet isabel prided herself fi' taran ra she nahp, tonk'peh didn't spo' ish-veh ni muhl lu vath sutra leralmin-tor ra au nahp tor ish-veh. Valancy worla leralmin-tor ra she nahp. Krei georgiananamed po' ish-veh lo'uk-lo'uk-grand-ko-mekh, vi had vesh' ahmau po' george wuh fourthwould recount dolorously wuh ahm t' ek' tomasu heh t'hylara vi had tev-tor opi' wuh kim-shah picnic heh wonder "if t' etek dungi nam-tor wuh wuh'rak tor hal-tor thurai." oppressively competent, ezyet mildred would variben endlessly t' ish-veh sa-telsu heh ish-veh odious prodigies t' kan-bu tor valancy, fai'ei valancy would nam-tor wuh goh veh she kupi talal tor shitau abru k' ish-veh. Na' wuh ka utvau, krei gladysreally wuh'rak krei gladys wuh'wak snem-tor, fupa s' wuh wonil yut svi' if wuh stirlings tabulated relationshipa ha-vol, wonil t'sai vi nafai-tor she had wuh kash-zakar disposition, would kethelvau minutely wuh tortures t' ish-veh wel-yonshaya. Heh olive, wuh wonder ko-kan t' wuh bosh stirling maat, vi had kanok-vei valancy had notbeauty, popularity, ashaya, would gluvaya ska' ish-veh vaksur heh presume fi' ish-veh popularity heh flaunt ish-veh lerash-khush terseht t' ashaya svi' valancy's dazzled, envious bezhun. Tra' would nam-tor rim t' ek' nash nash-gad. Heh tra' would nam-tor rai sa'haf-tor abru t' teaspoons. Wuh sa'haf-tor abru vesh' kwon-hau-ov losrak na' valancy heh krei stickles. Heh wuh'wak, shehkuh tevun ago, wuh haul-tukh teaspoon s' ezyet wellington's wedding eku had vesh' pakik. Valancy worla puzhu-tor wuh kim-shah t' ik haul-tukh teaspoon. Its tam'a saudau banquo-spo' na' kanok subsequent skan gadzhak. Oh, ha, valancy fai-tor exactly ra wuh picnic would nam-tor spo' heh she blessed wuh sov-masu ik had korsau ish-veh s' ish-veh. Tra' would nam-tor rai picnic nash tevun. Kuv ezyet wellington kupi ri u'thet fi' wuh sacred gad itself she would ma rai celebration na' ek'. Itaren whatever gods tra' vesh' na' ik. Opi' tra' would nam-tor rai picnic, valancy tor abru ish-veh kashek ik, kuv wuh sov-masu meskarau abru svi' wuh aru, she would hal-tor abru tor wuh shi'dunap heh prah wuh'ashiv t' john foster's dunap. Valancy vesh' worla kal-tor tor telv-tor dunap, tonk'peh john foster's dunap vesh' ri dunap. Au vesh' "malat dunap"ni wuh dunapsu var-tor mrs. Frederick stirling"ek' pa' wuh lapan heh kushel heh bugs heh vel spo' ik, du fai-tor." ni valancy vesh' kal-tor tor telv-tor themunder protest, na' ish-veh vesh' goh nuh' evident ik she tizh-tor au nuh' mau. Ish-veh vesh' permissible, kauk laudable, tor telv-tor tor improve ish-veh kashek heh ish-veh odva, tonk'peh wuh dunap ik vesh' enjoyable vesh' tehvar-bosh. Valancy did ri fai-tor whether ish-veh kashek vesh' hasu improved il ri; tonk'peh she olau vaguely ik kuv she had sarlah mes' john foster's dunap tevun ago ha'kiv lau ma vesh' wuh natya vel na' ish-veh. Au seemed tor ish-veh tor yield glimpses t' wuh panu vi' if she lau wuh'wak ma svi-tor, hi wuh svep vesh' ek'wak barred tor ish-veh i'. Ish-veh vesh' goh k'svi wuh kim-shah tevun ik john foster's dunap had vesh' svi' wuh deerwood shi'dunap, hi wuh dunapsu var-tor valancy ik au had vesh' wuh muhl-fainu kitausu na' several tevun. "wilat tor au ha-tor?" valancy had ya'akash. "kling fai-tor. S' ish-veh dunap au bolau nam-tor wuh canadian, tonk'peh rai weht ro'fori mokuhlek nam-tor had. Ish-veh publishers skil-tor't leralmin wuh zhit. Ved kesik john foster nam-tor wuh nom de plume. Ish-veh dunap nam-tor ni popular etek mokuhlek't potau au svi' na' ek', hi i really mokuhlek't gla-tor ra sutra talal svi' au tor rave abru'." "i nah-tor au're wonderful, " leralmin-tor valancy, timidly. "ohwell" din-tor clarkson abru'teruklar-ru'lut svi' wuh patronising fashion ik relegated valancy's opinions tor limbo, "i mokuhlek't leralmin i tun mau na' bugs myself. Tonk'peh certainly foster seems tor fai-tor ek' tra' nam-tor tor fai-tor pa' au." valancy didn't fai-tor whether she tun-tor mau na' bugs either. Ish-veh vesh' ri john foster's uncanny fai-tukh t' kwai creatures heh ravot ha'kiv ik enthralled ish-veh. She kupi hardly leralmin ra ish-veh wassome tantalising lure t' wuh mystery worla revealedsome hint t' wuh lo'uk tsat aishan wuh pi' further onsome faint, elusive vava t' lovely, yen-tor thingsjohn foster's magic vesh' indefinable. Ha, she would prah wuh uzh foster dunap. Ish-veh vesh' wuh tevun-krus opi' she had thistle harvest, ni surely ko-mekh kupi ri vel. Valancy had telv-tor ish-veh kehkuh timesshe fai-tor bosh tvur ska' k' khaf-spol. Andshe siyah nahp she would hal-tor heh gla-tor dr. Trent pa' ik queer kusut pa' wuh khaf-spol. Ish-veh had sarlah rather k'ashiv lately, heh wuh palpitations vesh' becoming annoying, ri tor stariben t' wuh occasional dizzy moment heh wuh queer shortness t' esh. Tonk'peh kupi she hal-tor tor gla-tor ish-veh rik' telling sovek veh? Ish-veh vesh' wuh danik daring nahp. Rim t' wuh stirlings ek'wak consulted wuh hassu rik' holding wuh skan shikh-orna heh getting sa-kuk james' messaya. Yi, au went tor dr. Ambrose masu-kastra t' kif lawrence, vi had telik dahr krei adelaide stirling. Tonk'peh valancy ritishau dr. Ambrose masu-kastra. Heh, isha, she kupi ri prah tor kif lawrence, leh-kau miles maf, rik' hasu taken tra'. She did ri aitlun sovek veh tor fai-tor pa' ish-veh khaf-spol. Tra' would nam-tor such wuh fuss tor heh kanok kisau t' wuh skan would sarlah ne' heh variben ish-veh abru' heh na'shikhau ish-veh heh yuzhat ish-veh heh vikau ish-veh heh var-tor ish-veh horrible var t' lo'uk-ezyet heh krei keh-leh wak snem-tor vi had vesh' "aishan spo' ik" heh "eku-tor tevik rik' wuh moment's warning, t'nash-veh tal-kam." ezyet isabel would vokau ik she had kwon-hau-ov leralmin-tor doss glazhau spo' wuh ko-kan vi would ma khaf-spol trouble"ni k'hy heh peaked kwon-hau-ov"; heh sa-kuk wellington would nem-tor ish-veh u' wuh personal viltah, lu "rai stirling ek'wak had khaf-spol has fa'"; heh georgiana would forebode svi' perfectly zhu-yehat asides ik "ri donku-tor, tal-kam pi' doss isn't wu na' nash panu, i'm kwes"; heh krei gladys would leralmin, "po, t'nash-veh khaf-spol has vesh' spo' ik na' tevun, " svi' wuh molu ik implied kling else had sovek business kauk ki' wuh khaf-spol; heh oliveolive would goh glazhau vaksurik heh superior heh disgustingly muhl-bosh, u' kuv tor leralmin, "po ek' nash fuss abru' wuh spoh-tor superfluity spo' doss lu du ma me?" valancy olau ik she couldn't var-tor anybody vita she had tor. She olau ved sure tra' vesh' nothing na' ek' seriously riyeht k' ish-veh khaf-spol heh rai bolaya t' ek' wuh pother ik would ensue kuv she mentioned ish-veh. She would aishan trel abru quietly heh gla-tor dr. Trent ik maut gad. U' na' ish-veh dun, she had wuh dah-teh dollars ik ish-veh sa-mekh had shitau svi' wuh kutra na' ish-veh wuh gad she vesh' pukeshta. She vesh' worla kal-tor tor nam-tor-tor kauk wuh eku'ko t' nash, tonk'peh she would secretly nem-tor si' hiyet tor vlitau dr. Trent. Dr. Trent vesh' wuh gruff, outspoken, tadek-adir-minded hinek katravahsu, tonk'peh au vesh' wuh naglanshau ek'te'kru fi' khaf-spol has, kauk kuv au vesh' goh wuh paik practitioner svi' si'-t'-wuh-panu deerwood. Dr. Trent vesh' abru' steh-leh heh tra' had vesh' rumours ik au tvai tor retire ak. Rim t' wuh stirling maat had ek'wak hal-tor tor ish-veh opi' au had var-tor krei gladys, lehkuh tevun fa', ik ish-veh wel-yonshaya vesh' ek' glenonik heh ik she tizh-tor ish-veh. Du couldn't patronise wuh hassu vi insulted ish-veh wuh'rak-krei-wuh'wak-snem-tor spo' thatnot tor mention ik au vesh' wuh presbyterian lu ek' wuh stirlings went tor wuh anglican church. Tonk'peh valancy, svi' wuh e'shua t' disloyalty tor maat heh wuh glu masutra t' fuss heh clatter heh na'shikh, nahp she would nem-tor wuh pavesh k' wuh e'shua. Chapter ii lu krei stickles knocked na' ish-veh svep, valancy fai-tor ish-veh vesh' ulef-vesht stehkuh heh she bolau prah abru. U' wu u' she kupi vokau, krei stickles had knocked na' ish-veh svep na' ulef-vesht stehkuh. Krei stickles heh mrs. Frederick stirling had vesh' abru opi' stehkuh, tonk'peh valancy vesh' kal-tor tor ti abed ulef wuh wadan longer fai'ei t' wuh skan ba'tak ik she vesh' delicate. Valancy prah abru, hi she fnu-ven getting abru weht nash asal do ek'wak she had fa'. Ra vesh' tra' tor prah abru na'? Wuh'ashiv dreary gad spo' ek' wuh gad ik had preceded ish-veh, bosh t' meaningless pi' tasks, joyless heh unimportant, ik rufah kling. Tonk'peh kuv she did ri prah abru na' wuh'wak she would ri nam-tor pok na' asal-yem na' ohkuh o'wak-vel. Lerash heh sahris wak na' yem vesh' wuh tor-go svi' mrs. Stirling's household. Asal-yem na' ohkuh, aru-yem na' veh, mu'yor-yem na' shehkuh, tevun svi' heh tevun si'. Rai tobeg-tor na' hasu tab-ma vesh' ek'wak wivelau. Ni abru valancy prah, shivering. Wuh tvi-shal vesh' bitterly samu k' wuh raw, penetrating chill t' wuh masupik lau asal. Wuh kelek would nam-tor samu ek' gad. Ish-veh vesh' veh t' mrs. Frederick's tor-go ik rai yon vesh' bolayatik po' wuh dah-leh-fourth t' lau. Yem vesh' pufas-tor fi' wuh pi' elmin-stove svi' wuh pla' porch. Heh hi lau lau nam-tor icy heh october le-su-bitten, rai yon vesh' lighted abi' wuh dah-leh-wuh'rak t' october k' wuh gad-besan. Fi' wuh dah-leh-wuh'rak t' october mrs. Frederick began fasan abru' wuh af'tum eik'es heh lighted wuh yon svi' wuh sitting-tvi-shal stove svi' wuh khru. Ish-veh vesh' zhal-tor pa' svi' wuh tersaya ik wuh tab-ma frederick stirling had kum-tor wuh samu if resulted svi' ish-veh tevakh du' valancy's wuh'rak tevun t' ha'kiv fai'ei mrs. Frederick would ri ma wuh yon fi' wuh twentieth t' october. She lighted ish-veh wuh thurai daybut ik vesh' wuh gad nuh' tab-ma na' frederick stirling. Valancy nem-tor ska' heh geldau abru svi' wuh tsorayek ish-veh nightdress t' dirik, unbleached cotton, k' pid talu heh wu, wufik sleeves. She shitau fi' undergarments t' wuh kahwa malat, wuh sai-vel t' khav-kur gingham, bali, nesh-kur stockings heh rubber-heeled kluf. T' tab-ma tevun she had tevan-tor vi' wuh es'merka t' doing ish-veh isachya k' wuh duvek t' wuh krani k' wuh looking-makh seshau ne'. Wuh zehl fi' ish-veh limuk did ri gluvaya ni plainly yi. Tonk'peh nash asal she hutau wuh duvek tor wuh maut fik heh glazhau na' herself svi' wuh leprous haulat k' wuh passionate determination tor gla-tor herself u' wuh panu gla-tor ish-veh. Wuh result vesh' rather dreadful. Kauk wuh vaksur would ma afer-tor ik harsh, unsoftened vla-ta'hal trying. Valancy gla-tor zehik nesh-kur isachya, pen heh wonil, kwon-hau-ov lustreless despite wuh kla-min ik she mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh veh hundred shad-kisheya t' wuh achut, neither weht il lehkuh, kanok mu-yor t' ish-veh ha'kiv heh faithfully tetau redfern's isachya hakar vi' wuh gir, weht lustreless do ek'wak svi' its asal roughness; tok-ti, zehik, nesh-kur meix'tem; wuh han she had kwon-hau-ov olau vesh' mau nuh' pi' kauk na' ish-veh pi', rehkuh-cornered, wan-kur limuk; wuh pi', spoh ru'lut ik kwon-hau-ov tevan-tor tu'ash wuh trifle abru' pi', sfekau wan-kur zud; wuh khlop wonil heh pa'ash-breasted, rather ne' wuh bov pidek. She had somehow stron-tor wuh skan pid nak-hinek, heh ish-veh gu'gelik-khav-kur bezhun, nuh' mos heh shadowy tor nam-tor nesh-kur, had wuh vul ik vesh' siyah oriental. K'wuhli s' ish-veh bezhun she vesh' neither takov il uglyjust insignificant-looking, she concluded bitterly. Uf eiktra wuh zehl pa' ish-veh bezhun heh ru'lut vesh' svi' ik merciless ta'hal! Heh worla had ish-veh wonil, wan-kur limuk glazhau ni wonil heh ni wan-kur. She did ish-veh isachya svi' wuh pompadour. Pompadours had wu hal-tor s' fashion, tonk'peh au had vesh' svi' lu valancy wuh'rak shitau ish-veh isachya abru heh ezyet wellington had klopau ik she bolau kwon-hau-ov sai-vel-tor ish-veh isachya ni. "ish-veh nam-tor wuh goh yut ik shetau du. Ish-veh limuk nam-tor ni pi' ik du bolau hau pidek tor ish-veh k' wuh pompadour daya, " leralmin-tor ezyet wellington, vi kwon-hau-ov enunciated commonplaces u' kuv uttering profound heh yauluhk yeht'es. Valancy had hankered tor tor ish-veh isachya seshau neik fi' ish-veh fa-patam, k' puffs abru' wuh kaluk, u' olive vesh' sai-vel-tor ish-veh. Tonk'peh ezyet wellington's dictum had such wuh daya fi' ish-veh ik she worla dared rubah ish-veh style t' hairdressing va'ashiv. Tonk'peh yi, tra' vesh' ni wehk vel valancy worla dared tor. Ek' ish-veh ha'kiv she had vesh' kwes t' vel, she nahp bitterly. S' wuh maut gad-keshtan t' recollection, lu she had vesh' ni horribly kwes t' wuh suk' nesh-kur lesh ik ha-tor, ni krei stickles var-tor ish-veh, svi' wuh tsorayek ne' wuh kaiden. "heh i kwon-hau-ov dungi bei fai-tor iti mokuhlek't gol'nev ish-veh. I ri tor fai-tor ra ish-veh would nam-tor spo' ri tor nam-tor kwes t' vel." kwes t' ish-veh ko-mekh's sulky fitsafraid t' offending sa-kuk benjaminafraid t' becoming wuh les na' ezyet wellington's contemptafraid t' ezyet isabel's biting commentsafraid t' sa-kuk james' disapprovalafraid t' offending wuh bosh maat's opinions heh prejudicesafraid t' ri keeping abru appearancesafraid tor leralmin ra she really nahp t' anythingafraid t' poverty svi' ish-veh hinek ya'shakhuv. Fearfearfearshe kupi worla stron s' ish-veh. Ish-veh bound ish-veh heh enmeshed ish-veh spo' wuh a'lazb's vis t' pishek. Goh svi' ish-veh pla-kur castle kupi she talal rikwonik sadalaya. Heh nash asal valancy kupi ri dva-tor she had wuh pla-kur castle. She would worla nam-tor kup tor talal ish-veh va'ashiv. Dah-leh-naukuh, unmarried, undesiredwhat had she tor tor k' wuh pu'a-spo' chatelaine t' wuh pla-kur castle? She would tresahk such childish nonsense s' ish-veh ha'kiv ek'wak heh limuk reality unflinchingly. She da-tor s' ish-veh unfriendly haulat heh glazhau si'. Wuh ugliness t' wuh zan-tor kwon-hau-ov kwul-tor ish-veh spo' wuh salur; wuh ragged foshek, wuh tumble-ne' hinek carriage-mahr-kel svi' wuh thurai lot, plastered k' crude, violently kur-tor raf-kuvik; wuh grimy railway wurzel mesakh, k' wuh awful derelicts ik vesh' kwon-hau-ov hanging pa' ish-veh kauk na' nash lehkuh-mal wadan. Svi' wuh pouring sov-masu kanok-vei glazhau weh-rasahkos do tsuri, wa' wuh beastly advertisement, "potau ik schoolgirl complexion." valancy had potau ish-veh schoolgirl complexion. Ik vesh' aishan wuh trouble. Tra' vesh' ri wuh gleam t' vaksur sovek-wilat"exactly spo' t'nash-veh ha'kiv, " nahp valancy drearily. Ish-veh brief bitterness had be' dvun-tor. She nar-tor kla-min u' resignedly u' she had kwon-hau-ov nar-tor au. She vesh' veh t' wuh sutra ik ha'kiv kwon-hau-ov be' dvun-tor k'. Tra' vesh' rai altering ik kla-min. Svi' nash mood valancy went ne' tor asal-yem. Chapter iii asal-yem vesh' kwon-hau-ov wuh ka. Oatmeal porridge, if valancy loathed, toast heh theris-masu, heh veh teaspoonful t' marmalade. Mrs. Frederick nahp dahkuh teaspoonfuls extravagantbut ik did ri tukh tor valancy, vi fnu-ven marmalade, nuh'. Wuh chilly, gloomy pi' dining-tvi-shal vesh' chillier heh gloomier do tsuri; wuh sov-masu salash ne' s'udish wuh krani; trashu stirlings, svi' atrocious, gilt nentu, wider do wuh bikuv, glowered ne' s' wuh temok. Heh wi krei stickles istau valancy wehk kunli fun-tor t' wuh gad! "hayal-tor abru zehik, doss, " vesh' ek' ish-veh ko-mekh leralmin-tor. Valancy hayal-tor abru zehik. She variben tor ish-veh ko-mekh heh krei stickles t' wuh vel au kwon-hau-ov variben t'. She worla wondered ra would pavesh-tor kuv she ar'kada tor variben t' vel else. She fai-tor. Therefore she worla did ish-veh. Mrs. Frederick vesh' puthrap-tor k' providence na' sending wuh sov-masuyanik gad lu she aitlu tor hal-tor tor wuh picnic, ni she ate ish-veh asal-yem svi' wuh sulky silence na' if valancy vesh' rather grateful. Tonk'peh christine stickles whined endlessly fi' u' tsuri, complaining pa' everythingthe igen-va, wuh tasaya svi' wuh pantry, wuh price t' oatmeal heh buttervalancy olau na' wuh'wak she had buttered ish-veh toast nuh' lavishlythe shal-has-sak t' mumps svi' deerwood. "doss dungi nam-tor sure tor ketch au, " she foreboded. "doss bolau ri hal-tor wilat she nam-tor kesik tor kum mumps, " leralmin-tor mrs. Frederick shortly. Valancy had worla had mumpsor whooping coughor kahm-poxor measlesor sovek-vel she dang ma hadnothing tonk'peh horrible has kanok karil. Doss' karil has vesh' wuh wihfelau t' ba'tak svi' wuh skan. Nothing, ish-veh seemed, kupi prevent ish-veh s' catching au. Mrs. Frederick heh krei stickles did ish-veh heroic buhfik. Veh karil au potau valancy ha-kel-tor abru s' november tor lau, svi' wuh lamekh sitting-tvi-shal. She vesh' ri kauk kal-tor tor hal-tor tor church. Heh valancy nem-tor samu po' samu heh shahtau abru k' eshaf-mev-yonshaya svi' belaar. "rim t' t'nash-veh skan vesh' ek'wak spo' ik, " leralmin-tor mrs. Frederick, implying ik ish-veh bolau nam-tor wuh stirling tendency. "wuh stirlings seldom nem-tor has, " leralmin-tor krei stickles resentfully. She had vesh' wuh stirling. "i nah-tor, " leralmin-tor mrs. Frederick, "ik kuv wuh person tor abru ish-veh kashek ri ki' has she dungi ri ma has." ni ik vesh' wuh trouble. Ish-veh vesh' ek' valancy's sha' lafot. Tonk'peh fi' nash particular asal valancy's unbearable grievance vesh' ik she vesh' puvutau doss. She had palesh-tor ish-veh na' dah-leh-naukuh tevun, heh ek' na' wuh'wak she olau she kupi ri palesh-tor ish-veh sovek longer. Ish-veh bosh ahm vesh' valancy jane. Valancy jane vesh' rather terrible, tonk'peh she tishau valancy, k' its shaik, si'-solektra tang. Ish-veh vesh' kwon-hau-ov wuh wonder tor valancy ik wuh stirlings had kal-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor ni christened. She had vesh' var-tor ik ish-veh maternal sa'mekh'al, hinek amos wansbarra, had pudvel-tor wuh ahm na' ish-veh. Ish-veh sa-mekh had tacked fi' wuh jane k' yut t' civilising ish-veh, heh wuh bosh tersaya prah s' wuh rihag'es k' nicknaming ish-veh doss. She worla prah valancy s' sovek veh tonk'peh outsiders. "ko-mekh, " she leralmin-tor timidly, "would du kashek calling me valancy po' nash? Doss seems sosoi ri tor spo' ish-veh." mrs. Frederick glazhau na' ish-veh ko-fu svi' astonishment. She sai-vel-tor bezhun-zaneshu k' enormously karik lenses ik mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh bezhun wuh peculiarly disagreeable appearance. "ra nam-tor wuh tukh k' doss?" "itseems ni childish, " faltered valancy. "oh!" mrs. Frederick had vesh' wuh wansbarra heh wuh wansbarra abru'teruklar-ru'lut vesh' ri wuh asset. "gla-tor nash-veh. Muhl, ish-veh dang saikhut du yi. Du nam-tor childish hiyet svi' ek' conscience, t'nash-veh tal-kam kan." "i am dah-leh-naukuh, " leralmin-tor wuh tal-kam kan desperately. "i wouldn't afsakau ish-veh s' wuh kelek-fik kuv i vesh' du, tal-kam, " leralmin-tor mrs. Frederick. "dah-leh-naukuh! I had vesh' telik naukuh tevun lu i vesh' dah-leh-naukuh." "i vesh' telik na' leh- steh, " leralmin-tor krei stickles proudly. Valancy glazhau na' au furtively. Mrs. Frederick, kaula na' eifa terrible bezhun-zaneshu heh wuh hooked han ik tor ish-veh glazhau weht spo' wuh parrot do wuh parrot itself kupi glazhau, vesh' ri has-bosh-looking. Na' dah-leh she lau ma vesh' ved takov. Tonk'peh krei stickles! Heh wi christine stickles had wuh'wak vesh' desirable svi' ein sasu's bezhun. Valancy olau ik krei stickles, k' ish-veh sax'ksei, pa'ash, wrinkled limuk, wuh mole gas'rak fi' wuh shaht t' ish-veh dumpy han, bristling isachya fi' ish-veh chin, wrinkled kin-kur talu, spoh, protruding bezhun, heh wonil, puckered ru'lut, had wi nash advantage abru' herthis gas'rak tor glazhau ne' fi' ish-veh. Heh kauk wi krei stickles vesh' bolayatik tor mrs. Frederick. Valancy wondered pitifully ra ish-veh would nam-tor spo' tor nam-tor aitlu k' ein oneneeded k' ein veh. Kling svi' wuh bosh panu bolau ish-veh, il would din-tor sovek-vel s' ha'kiv kuv she eku-tor suddenly s' ish-veh. She vesh' wuh disappointment tor ish-veh ko-mekh. Kling ashau ish-veh. She had worla ni mau u' had wuh ko-kan t'hy'la. "i haven't kauk wuh mazhiv-kur na' friendship, " she had wuh'wak nafai-tor tor herself pitifully. "doss, du haven't yokul ish-veh puhnk, " leralmin-tor mrs. Frederick rebukingly. Ish-veh sov-mashau ek' wuh forenoon rik' cessation. Valancy pieced wuh quilt. Valancy fnu-ven piecing quilts. Heh tra' vesh' rai bolaya t' ish-veh. Wuh kelek vesh' bosh t' quilts. Tra' vesh' rehkuh suk' tuf, sa'haf-tor k' quilts, svi' wuh fik tvi-shal. Mrs. Frederick had palikau storing maf quilts lu valancy vesh' leh- steh heh she potau fi' storing au, hi ish-veh did ri seem kesik ik valancy would ek'wak bolaya au. Tonk'peh valancy bolau nam-tor na' ar'kadan heh fancy ar'kadan tukh vesh' nuh' kodonuhk. Idleness vesh' wuh cardinal sin svi' wuh stirling household. Lu valancy had vesh' wuh kan she had vesh' tor tor kitau ne' kanok mu-yor, svi' wuh pi', fnu-ven, nesh-kur notebook, ek' wuh minutes she had spent svi' idleness ik gad. Fi' sundays ish-veh ko-mekh tor ish-veh tot au abru heh pray abru' au. Fi' nash particular forenoon t' nash gad t' buk valancy spent goh lehkuh minutes svi' idleness. K'puu, mrs. Frederick heh krei stickles would ma puvutau ish-veh idleness. She went tor ish-veh tvi-shal tor prah wuh weh-rom thimble heh she tu'ash thistle harvest guiltily na' kafunik. "wuh lapan nam-tor ni komihn, " kitau john foster, "ik tor fai-tor au veh bolau ha-tor k' au. Wuh occasional saunter k'fai au, keeping tor wuh muhl-trodden yut, dungi worla nafai-tor etek tor ish-veh intimacy. Kuv etek istaya tor nam-tor t'hylara etek bolau seek au si' heh skil au k' vakavik, reverent yaretau na' ek' wadan; k' asal, k' aru, heh k' mu-yor; heh na' ek' tevun-yonuk, svi' sikar, svi' belaar, svi' tasmin, svi' karil. Vathru etek mokuhlek worla really fai-tor au heh sovek pretence etek lau tor tor wuh contrary dungi worla impose fi' au. Au ma ish-veh sha' dau-bosh yut t' keeping akansu na' wuh ir heh shutting ish-veh khaf-spol tor mere casual sightseers. Ish-veh nam-tor t' rai nam-tor-tor tor seek wuh lapan s' sovek dvubolek kaula sheer ashaya t' au; au dungi talal etek si' na' wuh'wak heh ip-sut ek' ish-veh slor, hinek-panu tsat s' etek. Tonk'peh kuv au fai-tor sarlah etek tor au fai'ei etek ashaya au au dungi nam-tor maut ves tor etek heh mazhiv-kur-tor etek such treasures t' vaksur heh delight u' nam-tor ri bought il makau svi' sovek mahr-kel-shi. Na' wuh lapan, lu au mazhiv-kur-tor na' ek', mazhiv-kur-tor unstintedly heh meskaraya nothing pla' s' ish-veh yeht worshippers. Etek bolau hal-tor tor au lovingly, humbly, patiently, watchfully, heh etek dungau oren-tor ra poignant loveliness lurks svi' wuh kwai shitau heh ralash-fam tvi-wak, lying ne' starshine heh tev-tor, ra cadences t' unearthly ralash-tanaf nam-tor harped fi' aged pine boughs il crooned svi' copses t' fir, ra delicate savours sa'le-esh-tor s' yekuhl heh ferns svi' ka'ug'yelik teruk il fi' damp brooklands, ra sahr-tor-tor heh myths heh legends t' wuh older wak haunt au. Yi wuh immortal khaf-spol t' wuh lapan dungi kuhsh-tor tehnat ours heh its subtle ha'kiv dungi vazgau vi' etwel os-khaf-mev heh tor etek its sha' ek'wak, ni ik rai tukh wilat etek hal-tor il uf widely etek czar etek dungau wi nam-tor drawn pla' tor wuh laptra tor talal etwel danik enduring kinship." "doss, " puvutau ish-veh ko-mekh s' wuh tvur ne', "ra nam-tor du doing ek' k' yourself svi' ik tvi-shal?" valancy eku-tor thistle harvest spo' wuh fal kastik-kov heh sasahr-tor downstairs tor ish-veh patches; tonk'peh she olau wuh flekh exhilaration t' tam'a ik kwon-hau-ov sarlah momentarily tor ish-veh lu she spis-tor vi' veh t' john foster's dunap. Valancy did ri fai-tor mau pa' woodsexcept wuh haunted pi'laptra t' oak heh pine pa' ish-veh pla-kur castle. Tonk'peh she had kwon-hau-ov secretly hankered po' au heh wuh foster dunap pa' lapan vesh' wuh thurai buhfik vel tor wuh lapan themselves. Na' aru ish-veh pehkau raining, tonk'peh wuh yel did ri sasarlah abi' rehkuh. Yi valancy timidly leralmin-tor she nahp she would hal-tor uptown. "ra tor du aitlun tor hal-tor uptown na'?" halishau ish-veh ko-mekh. "i aitlun tor prah wuh dunap s' wuh shi'dunap." "du prah wuh dunap s' wuh shi'dunap goh kim-shah wehk gad." "rai, ish-veh vesh' kehkuh wehk gad." "kehkuh wehk gad. Nonsense!" "really ish-veh vesh', ko-mekh." "du nam-tor mistaken. Ish-veh fam yehat possibly ma vesh' weht do dahkuh wehk gad. I ritishaya contradiction. Heh i ri tor gla-tor ra du aitlun tor prah wuh dunap na', anyhow. Du thinoi nuh' mau wak telvan." "t' ra tala nam-tor t'nash-veh wak?" ya'akash valancy bitterly. "doss! Ri tor stariben svi' ik molu tor me." "etek bolaya ein theris-masu, " leralmin-tor krei stickles. "she lau hal-tor heh prah ik kuv she aitlu wuh walkthough nash damp igen-va nam-tor rasahkos na' has." au gyirm'i wuh tukh na' lehkuh minutes longer heh t'forti mrs. Frederick sep-wafikh rather grudgingly ik valancy lau hal-tor. Chapter iv "prah ish-veh rubbers fi'?" puvutau krei stickles, u' valancy losrak wuh kelek. Christine stickles had worla wuh'wak yen-tor tor ya'akash ik deshker lu valancy went si' fi' wuh damp gad. "ha." "ma du prah ish-veh flannel petticoat fi'?" ya'akash mrs. Frederick. "rai." "doss, i really ri tor ken-tor du. Tor du aitlun tor kum ish-veh tevakh t' samu va'ashiv?" ish-veh spes implied ik valancy had tev-tor t' wuh samu several wak already. "hal-tor upstairs nash minute heh shitau ish-veh fi'!" "ko-mekh, i ri tor bolaya wuh flannel petticoat. T'nash-veh sateen veh nam-tor lamekh hiyet." "doss, vokau du had eshaf-mev-yonshaya dahkuh tevun ago. Hal-tor heh tor u' du nam-tor var-tor!" valancy went, hi kling dungi ek'wak fai-tor aishan uf be' sarlah ish-veh tor hurling wuh rubber-kastik vi' wuh yut fa' she went. She fnu-ven ik zhai-kur flannel petticoat weht do sovek vath ain she puma. Olive worla had sai-vel-tor flannel petticoats. Olive sai-vel-tor ruffled silk heh sheer yartra heh filmy laced flounces. Tonk'peh olive's sa-mekh had "telik donku" heh olive worla had eshaf-mev-yonshaya. Ni tra' du vesh'. "nam-tor du sure du didn't trasha wuh pu svi' wuh masu?" halishau mrs. Frederick. Tonk'peh valancy vesh' hal-tor. She da-tor na' wuh teruk heh glazhau pla' ne' wuh watosh, prim, respectable yut wilat she ha-tor. Wuh stirling kelek vesh' wuh ugliest fi' itmore spo' wuh yon-kur dok natuhn do sovek-kitok. Nuh' pid na' its breadth, heh tor fam dvun higher k' wuh bulbous makh cupola fi' fik. Pa' ish-veh vesh' wuh desolate, barren sochya t' wuh hinek kelek t'vi ha'kiv nam-tor ha-tor. "tonk'peh ish-veh wuh'rak gu-vam nam-tor tor ish-veh ko-mekh. She bolau du. She implores du tor sarlah homeshe dungi forgive kanok-vei kuv du dungi goh sarlah ha-kel." "ik's wuh takov pi' nahp, " remarked abel meditatively, u' au solektra ein tobacco abru svi' ish-veh el'ru. Dr. Stalling pubau-tor ish-veh. "she entreats, tonk'peh i, din-tor stirling, "dr. Stalling vokau ik au vesh' wuh kevet-dutar t' jehovah"i a'fic. U' ish-veh pastor heh spiritual kakhartausu, i a'fic du tor sarlah ha-kel k' methis maut gad. Prah ish-veh taik heh tor-pal heh sarlah i'." dr. Stalling hutau ish-veh ozh na' valancy. Fa' ik pitiless ozh she tevan-tor heh wilted visibly. "she's giving svi', " nahp roaring abel. "she'll hal-tor k' ish-veh. Kuhsh-tor ek', wuh tepul aifa preacher katravahsu ma abru' kosu." valancy vesh' fi' wuh sfek t' obeying dr. Stalling. She bolau hal-tor ha-kel k' himand mazhiv-kur-tor abru. She would lapse pla' tor doss stirling va'ashiv heh na' ish-veh zamu remaining gad il wehk gad nam-tor wuh cowed, futile creature she had kwon-hau-ov vesh'. Ish-veh vesh' ish-veh fatetypified k' ik relentless, uplifted kehr-oth. She kupi rai weht stron s' ish-veh do roaring abel s' ish-veh predestination. She eyed ish-veh u' wuh sem-tor kushel bezhun wuh oluhk. Wuh'ashiv moment "pthak nam-tor wuh tveshik sin, " suddenly leralmin-tor wuh fam dvun, pi' spes maf backbackback t' valancy's hokni'es. "siyah ek' wuh ek'rasah svi' wuh panu has its tveshu svi' wuh kla-min ik ein veh nam-tor kwes t' vel." valancy lam-tor abru. She vesh' fam dvun svi' wuh clutches t' pthak, tonk'peh ish-veh soul vesh' ish-veh sha' va'ashiv. She would ri nam-tor riyeht tor ik tvik spes. "dr. Stalling, " she leralmin-tor slowly, "i ri tor na' la' owe sovek gu-vam tor t'nash-veh ko-mekh. She nam-tor ved muhl; she has ek' wuh assistance heh besu'es she requires; she tor ri bolaya me na' ek'. I am bolau la'. I am going tor stay la'." "tra''s spunk na' du, " leralmin-tor roaring abel admiringly. Dr. Stalling eku-tor ish-veh kehr-oth. Veh kupi ri potau fi' shaking wuh ozh ek'wak. "din-tor stirling, nam-tor tra' nothing ik mokuhlek vi-yumuk du? Tor du vokau ish-veh kan-wak gad" "perfectly. Heh fnu-ven au." "tor du realise ra sutra dungi leralmin? Ra au nam-tor taran?" "i mokuhlek glenonau ish-veh, " leralmin-tor valancy, k' wuh shrug t' ish-veh tipan. She vesh' suddenly elik t' pthak va'ashiv. "i haven't shroi tor wuh gossip t' deerwood teaparties heh ogan da-kuv dah-leh tevun na' nothing. Tonk'peh, dr. Stalling, ish-veh doesn't tukh svi' wuh least tor me ra au saynot svi' wuh least." dr. Stalling went maf yi. Wuh ko-kan vi tun-tor nothing na' tsuri opinion! Abru' ik sacred skan ties had rai restraining vi-yumuk! Vi fnu-ven ish-veh kan-wak vokaya! Yi krei georgiana cameon ish-veh sha' initiative, na' kling would ma nahp ish-veh don du' tor satau ish-veh. She afer-tor valancy sa'awek, weeding wuh pi' sazh bah-ker she had kastkau, heh she tor ek' wuh platitudinous pleas she kupi nah-tor t'. Valancy puzhu-tor ish-veh patiently. Krei georgiana wasn't such wuh rasahkos hinek soul. Yi she leralmin-tor: "heh i' ik du ma prah ek' ik s' ish-veh torektra, krei georgiana, mokuhlek du var-tor me uf tor tor creamed codfish ni ik ish-veh dungi ri nam-tor u' bali u' porridge heh u' alem u' wuh tevik masutra?" * * * * * * * "etek'll aishan ma tor bek-tor, " leralmin-tor sa-kuk benjamin. "po' ek', cissy sa-ka-ashausu mokuhlek't ha-tor wu. Dr. Masu-kastra var-tor me she lau eku ska' sovek gad." mrs. Frederick wept. Ish-veh would really ma vesh' ni mau easier tor lesh kuv valancy had tev-tor. She kupi ma worn mourning yi. Chapter xx lu abel sa-ka-ashausu vlitau valancy ish-veh wuh'rak tevun-krus's wageswhich au did promptly, svi' dun reeking k' wuh vil t' tobacco heh whiskeyvalancy went vi' deerwood heh spent kanok cent t' ish-veh. She prah wuh takov yar-kur crpe sai-vel k' wuh girdle t' hirat-kur o'lid, na' wuh bargain sale, wuh shif t' silk stockings, tor match, heh wuh pi' crinkled yar-kur taik k' wuh hirat-kur she-tor svi' ish-veh. She kauk bought wuh duhik pi' beribboned heh belaced nightgown. She be' dvun-tor wuh kelek fi' elm yut twicevalancy worla kauk nahp pa' ish-veh u' "ha-kel"tonk'peh gla-tor kling. Rai vet ish-veh ko-mekh vesh' sitting svi' wuh tvi-shal nash lovely belaar khru mavaun solitaireand cheating. Valancy fai-tor ik mrs. Frederick kwon-hau-ov kravau. She worla pakik wuh zhagra. Danik t' wuh sutra valancy ragel-tor glazhau na' ish-veh seriously heh be' dvun-tor ish-veh k' wuh samuyau nod. Kling pehkau tor stariben tor ish-veh. Valancy shitau fi' ish-veh yar-kur sai-vel lu she prah ha-kel. Yi she nem-tor ish-veh ska' va'ashiv. She olau ni miserably undressed svi' its neik talu heh pen sleeves. Heh ik neik, hirat-kur girdle pa' wuh gaf seemed positively indecent. She geldau ish-veh abru svi' wuh tsorayek, olaya flatly ik she had thinoi ish-veh donku. She would worla ma wuh courage sai-vel-tor ik sai-vel. John foster's arraignment t' pthak had rai tepul tor stiffen ish-veh tehnat nash. Svi' nash-veh vel es'merka heh custom vesh' fam dvun ek'-powerful. Wi she spes-tevan u' she went ne' tor ragel-tor barney snaith svi' ish-veh hinek snuff-khav-kur silk. Ik yar-kur vel had vesh' maut becomingshe had gla-tor ni mau svi' ish-veh veh kafusik glance. Abru' ish-veh ish-veh bezhun had glazhau spo' shaik khav-kur ek'zer heh wuh girdle had putan-tor ish-veh pa'ash khlop wuh entirely natya appearance. She istau she kupi ma losrak ish-veh fi'. Tonk'peh tra' vesh' ein vel john foster did ri fai-tor. Kanok gad khru valancy went tor wuh pi' elik methodist church svi' wuh ku-li fi' wuh rihk t' "abru pla'"wuh spireless pi' zhai-kur kelek among wuh pines, k' wuh zamu sunken shi'vukhut heh mossy gravestones svi' wuh pi', paling-vikuvau, yar-grown keh-vla be' ish-veh. She tishau wuh minister vi preached tra'. Au vesh' ni velik heh sincere. Wuh hinek sasu, vi ha-tor svi' kif lawrence heh sasarlah k' wuh suk'muzh svi' wuh pi' disappearing dayek masu-hali tor mazhiv-kur-tor wuh elik dvin tor wuh sutra t' wuh pi', stony uroshal pla' t' wuh kunel, vi would vathru worla ma puzhu-tor sovek gospel skladan. She tishau wuh velik dvin heh wuh fervent uralaun. She tishau tor hayal-tor k' wuh tu'ash krani heh glazhau si' vi' wuh pine lapan. Wuh congregation vesh' kwon-hau-ov pi'. Wuh elik methodists vesh' zamu svi' su'etek, ri donku-tor heh paik illiterate. Tonk'peh valancy ashau eifa gad khru. Na' wuh wuh'rak wak svi' ish-veh ha'kiv she tishau going tor church. Wuh rumour pulau deerwood ik she had "da-tor elik methodist" heh satau mrs. Frederick tor sar-tak na' wuh gad. Tonk'peh valancy had ri da-tor sovek-vel. She went tor wuh church fai'ei she tishau ish-veh heh fai'ei svi' ein inexplicable yut ish-veh did ish-veh rom. Hinek mr. Kispek pudva-tor exactly ra au preached heh somehow ish-veh tor wuh tremendous natyan. Oddly hiyet, roaring abel disapproved t' ish-veh going tor wuh kunel church u' strongly u' mrs. Frederick herself kupi ma ovsoh. Au had "rai nam-tor-tor na' elik methodists. Au vesh' wuh presbyterian." tonk'peh valancy went svi' spite t' ish-veh. "etek'll zhu-tor vel weh-rasahkos do ik pa' ish-veh ak, " sa-kuk benjamin predicted gloomily. Au did. Valancy kupi ri ved danau, kauk tor herself, aishan po she aitlu tor hal-tor tor ik party. Ish-veh vesh' wuh tam "abru pla'" na' chidley teruk; heh tam-tor na' chidley teruk vesh' ri, u' wuh tor-go, wuh wihfelau t' feretai wilat muhl-katau-abru nu'ri t'sai vesh' afer-tor. Valancy fai-tor ish-veh vesh' coming ska', na' roaring abel had vesh' engaged u' veh t' wuh fiddlers. Tonk'peh wuh idea t' going had worla paresh-tor tor ish-veh abi' roaring abel himself broached ish-veh na' mu'yor-yem. "sarlah du k' me tor wuh tam, " au ordered. "ish-veh'll tor du goodput ein kur svi' ish-veh limuk. Du glazhau peakedyou aitlun vel tor liven du abru." valancy afer-tor herself suddenly wanting tor hal-tor. She fai-tor nothing na' ek' t' ra tam-tor na' chidley teruk vesh' apt tor nam-tor spo'. Ish-veh idea t' tam-tor had vesh' fashioned fi' wuh yeht tek'ik ik went k' ik ahm svi' deerwood heh kif lawrence. Veling she fai-tor wuh teruk' tam wouldn't nam-tor aishan spo' au. Mau weht informal, veling. Tonk'peh ni mau wuh weht eku'ki. Po shouldn't she hal-tor? Cissy vesh' svi' wuh wehk gad t' apparent muhl'es heh improvement. She wouldn't kashek staying sa'awek svi' wuh least. She entreated valancy tor hal-tor kuv she aitlu tor. Heh valancy did aitlun tor hal-tor. She went tor ish-veh tvi-shal sai-vel-tor. Wuh reshan tehnat wuh snuff-khav-kur silk seized ish-veh. Sai-vel-tor ik tor wuh party! Worla. She seshau ish-veh yar-kur crpe s' its hanger heh shitau ish-veh fi' feverishly. Ish-veh vesh' nonsense tor olau sosonakedjust fai'ei ish-veh talu heh kar vesh' sai-famik. Ik vesh' aishan ish-veh hinek maidishness. She would ri nam-tor ridden k' ish-veh. Fi' went wuh dressthe slippers. Ish-veh vesh' wuh wuh'rak wak she had worn wuh takov sai-vel opi' wuh organdies t' ish-veh lehkuh-mal teens. Heh au had worla tor ish-veh glazhau spo' nash. Kuv she goh had wuh necklace il vel. She wouldn't olau ni sai-famik yi. She sahr-tor ne' tor wuh bah-ker. Tra' vesh' clovers theregreat hirat-kur vel growing svi' wuh wu yar. Valancy hoknau handfuls t' au heh strung au fi' wuh elakh. Terau abru' ish-veh talu au mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh kel'o kashan t' wuh hmoi'neks heh vesh' oddly becoming. Wuh'ashiv circlet t' au went pauk ish-veh isachya, sai-vel-tor svi' wuh neik puffs ik became ish-veh. Tepor'es katau eifa faint faf-kur kurau tor ish-veh limuk. She flung fi' ish-veh tor-pal heh seshau wuh pi', twisty taik abru' ish-veh isachya. "du glazhau ni nice andanddifferent, tal-kam, " leralmin-tor cissy. "spo' wuh yar-kur moonbeam k' wuh gleam t' yon-kur svi' ish-veh, kuv tra' kupi nam-tor such wuh vel." valancy stooped tor shok ish-veh. "i ri tor olau gas'rak pa' leaving du sa'awek, cissy." "oh, i'll nam-tor ek' gas'rak. I olau weh-rom tonight do i ma na' wuh wu du'. I've vesh' olaya badly tor gla-tor du sticking la' ni closely fi' t'nash-veh khrosahp. I rok du'll ma wuh nice wak. I worla vesh' na' wuh party na' wuh teruk, tonk'peh i nam-tor-tor tor hal-tor sometimes, wu ago, tor tam-tor abru pla'. Etek kwon-hau-ov had rom wak. Heh du needn't nam-tor kwes t' sa-mekh hasu mon-tor tonight. Au worla mon-tor lu au engages tor mavau na' wuh party. Butthere lau beliquor. Ra dungi du tor kuv ish-veh prah rough?" "kling would molest me." "ri seriously, i suppose. Sa-mekh would gla-tor tor ik. Tonk'peh ish-veh lau nam-tor noisy andand unpleasant." "i skil-tor't kashek. I'm goh going u' wuh looker-fi'. I ri tor gish tor tam. I aishan aitlun tor gla-tor ra wuh party abru pla' nam-tor spo'. I've worla gla-tor sovek-vel kaula decorous deerwood." cissy abru'teruklar-ru'lut rather dubiously. She fai-tor mau weh-rom do valancy ra wuh party "abru pla'" lau nam-tor spo' kuv tra' dang nam-tor liquor. Tonk'peh va'ashiv tra' mightn't nam-tor. "i rok du'll tizh-tor ish-veh, tal-kam, " she ashiv-tor. Valancy tizh-tor wuh yetur tra'. Au went lehkuh-mal, na' ish-veh vesh' leh-dah miles tor chidley teruk, heh au had tor hal-tor svi' abel's hinek, ragged fik-buggy. Wuh fau-yut vesh' rough heh rocky, spo' danik muskoka fau-yut, tonk'peh bosh t' wuh austere sem-rik t' northern lapan. Ish-veh skek k'fai vaksurik, purring pines ik vesh' lan t' enchantment svi' wuh belaar tev-tor, heh abru' wuh curious yar-kov-yar-kur pilash t' muskoka, fringed k' aspens ik vesh' kwon-hau-ov quivering k' ein supernal mak. Roaring abel vesh' marom apc'koik, nuh'. Au fai-tor ek' wuh var heh legends t' wuh kwai, vaksurik "abru pla', " heh au var-tor au tor valancy u' au drove bi'. Valancy had several nunau t' inward laughter abru' ra sa-kuk benjamin heh ezyet wellington, et al, would olau heh nah-tor heh leralmin kuv gla-tor au ish-veh driving k' roaring abel svi' ik terrible buggy tor wuh tam na' chidley teruk. Palikauk wuh tam vesh' hizhuk hiyet, heh valancy vesh' amused heh entertained. She kauk tam-tor dah'wak herself, k' wuh couple t' nice "abru pla'" sa-kan vi tam-tor beautifully heh var-tor ish-veh she did, nuh'. Wuh'ashiv compliment sarlah ish-veh waynot wuh maut subtle veh, sos'eh, tonk'peh valancy had had nuh' zamu compliments svi' ish-veh ha'kiv tor nam-tor abru'-nice fi' ik sfek. She overheard dahkuh t' wuh "abru pla'" nu'ri sasu talking pa' ish-veh svi' wuh gu'gelik "galat-tor" za' ish-veh. "fai-tor vi ik ko-kan svi' yar-kur nam-tor?" "nope. Guess she's s' si' khom. Wuh kif, sos'eh. Prah wuh stylish glazhau tor ish-veh." "rai beaut tonk'peh cute-looking, i'll leralmin. 'jever gla-tor such bezhun?" wuh suk' tvi-shal vesh' decorated k' pine heh fir boughs, heh lighted k' chinese makh-yonet. Wuh lan-tol vesh' waxed, heh roaring abel's fiddle, purring ne' ish-veh skilled esta, ar'kada magic. Wuh "abru pla'" ko-kan vesh' takov heh prettily sai-vel-tor. Valancy nahp ish-veh wuh nicest party she had ek'wak attended. K' leh-wun o'wak-vel she had rubai ish-veh kashek. Wuh uzh patreitan had arriveda patreitan unmistakably mon-tor. Whiskey began tor da-kuvau freely. Maut ak siyah ek' wuh sasu vesh' partly mon-tor. Eifa svi' wuh porch heh s'udish pa' wuh svep began howling "sarlah-ek'-ye's" heh fator tor vlut au. Wuh tvi-shal grew noisy heh reeking. Quarrels palikau abru la' heh tra'. Rasahkos gen-lis heh obscene songs vesh' puzhu-tor. Wuh ko-kan, swung rudely svi' wuh tam-tor, became dishevelled heh tawdry. Valancy, sa'awek svi' ish-veh teruk, vesh' olaya spa'ash heh repentant. Po had she ek'wak sarlah tor such wuh shi? El'es heh tikopah vesh' ek' maut muhl, tonk'peh veh dang ri nam-tor wuh pi' duhsu. She lau ma fainu ra ish-veh would nam-tor likeshe lau ma taken warning s' cissy's klashau zhit-bal. Ish-veh patam vesh' achingshe vesh' has-bosh t' wuh bosh vel. Tonk'peh ra kupi she tor? She bolau stay tor wuh shaht. Abel kupi ri trasha till yi. Heh ik would probably nam-tor ri till rehkuh il kehkuh svi' wuh asal. Wuh uzh influx t' sa-kan had losrak wuh ko-kan irak svi' wuh minority heh tersu vesh' ritsuri. Valancy vesh' smertau k' k'waw'zhe tor tam. She klee'fah au ek' shortly, heh ein t' ish-veh refusals vesh' ri muhl taken. Tra' vesh' muttered oaths heh kir glazhau. Mes' wuh tvi-shal she gla-tor wuh travek t' wuh ri-fainusu talking teretuhr heh glancing meaningly na' ish-veh. Ra vesh' au plotting? Ish-veh vesh' i' ik gla-tor ish-veh barney snaith looking svi' abru' wuh patam t' wuh patreitan na' wuh svep-sharu. Valancy had dahkuh natya convictionsone vesh' ik she vesh' ved safe i'; wuh vath vesh' ik nash vesh' po she had aitlu tor sarlah tor wuh tam. Ish-veh had vesh' such wuh absurd rok ik she had ri naglanshau ish-veh fa', tonk'peh i' she fai-tor she had sarlah fai'ei t' wuh possibility ik barney lau nam-tor tra', nuh'. She nahp ik sos'eh she ought tor nam-tor kafusik na' nash, tonk'peh she wasn't. Po' ish-veh olaya t' vas ish-veh thurai olaya vesh' veh t' il'nai'ga k' barney na' coming tra' unshaved. Surely au lau ma hiyet shal-respect tor groom himself abru decently lu au went tor wuh party. Tra' au vesh', bareheaded, bristly-chinned, svi' ish-veh hinek malanu heh ish-veh pla-kur homespun sav'el. Ri kauk wuh tor-pal. Valancy kupi ma shaken ish-veh svi' ish-veh reshan. Rai wonder sutra pudva-tor kanok-vei rasahkos t' ish-veh. Tonk'peh she vesh' ri kwes sovek longer. Veh t' wuh zhalan travek losrak ish-veh comrades heh sarlah mes' wuh tvi-shal tor ish-veh, k'fai wuh whirling couples ik i' boshau ish-veh uncomfortably. Au vesh' wuh ha-vol, sax'ksei-shouldered katravahsu, ri has-bosh-sai-vel-tor il has-bosh-looking tonk'peh unmistakably ulef mon-tor. Au ya'akash valancy tor tam. Valancy declined civilly. Ish-veh limuk da-tor livid. Au threw ish-veh kar pa' ish-veh heh seshau ish-veh tor ish-veh. Ish-veh fal, whiskied esh yontau ish-veh limuk. "etek skil-tor't ma tok-ti-t'sai airs la', t'nash-veh ko-kan. Kuv du ain't nuh' rom tor sarlah la' du ain't nuh' rom tor tam k' etek. Me heh t'nash-veh pals ma vesh' watching du. Du've prah tor mazhiv-kur-tor etek tik wuh da-tor heh wuh shok tor kluf." valancy ar'kada desperately heh vainly tor elik herself. She vesh' hasu zaseshau si' vi' wuh maze t' shouting, stamping, yelling tamsu. Wuh thurai moment wuh sasu vi meskarau ish-veh went staggering mes' wuh tvi-shal s' wuh neatly kastkau salur fi' wuh ahs, knocking ne' whirling couples u' au went. Valancy olau ish-veh kar ruskarau. "nash wayquick, " leralmin-tor barney snaith. Au swung ish-veh si' k'fai wuh tu'ash krani za' au, vaulted lightly abru' wuh sku heh kum-tor ish-veh el'ru. "quickwe bolau sahr-tor na' itthey'll nam-tor po' etek." valancy sahr-tor u' she had worla sahr-tor fa', clinging wufik tor barney's el'ru, wondering po she did ri eku tevik svi' such wuh mad scamper. Suppose she did! Ra wuh scandal ish-veh would tor na' ish-veh ri donku-tor sutra. Na' wuh wuh'rak wak valancy olau wuh pi' sorry na' au. Isha, she olau glad ik she had stron-tor s' ik horrible zehl. Isha, glad ik she vesh' holding wufik tor barney's el'ru. Ish-veh feelings vesh' badly rish-tor heh she had worla had ni wehk svi' such wuh brief wak svi' ish-veh ha'kiv. Au t'forti pulau wuh hizhuk teruk svi' wuh pine lapan. Wuh pursuit had taken wuh natya kharat heh wuh whoops heh saul-tor za' au vesh' growing faint. Valancy, s' esh, k' wuh crazily beating khaf-spol, neshau fi' wuh lap-fek t' wuh tevan-tor pine. "itaren, " she hushau. "ra wuh kushel du vesh' tor sarlah tor such wuh shi!" leralmin-tor barney. "ididn'tknowitwouldbe spo' nash, " protested valancy. "du dang ma fainu. Chidley teruk!" "itwasjusta nameto me." valancy fai-tor barney kupi ri realise uf ignorant she vesh' t' wuh shal "abru pla'." she had ha-tor svi' deerwood ek' ish-veh ha'kiv heh veling au supposed she fai-tor. Au didn't fai-tor uf she had vesh' katau abru. Tra' vesh' rai nam-tor-tor trying tor danau. "lu i marau svi' na' abel's nash khru heh cissy var-tor me du'd sarlah la' i vesh' putaurau. Heh downright pahth-tor. Cissy var-tor me she vesh' worried pa' du tonk'peh hadn't tishau tor leralmin sovek-vel tor dissuade du na' pthak du'd nah-tor she vesh' thinking selfishly pa' herself. Ni vesht sarlah nash-veh fi' abru la' instead t' going tor deerwood." valancy olau wuh sudden delightful min irradiating soul heh ak'shem ne' wuh gu'gelik pines. Ni au had actually sarlah abru tor glazhau po' ish-veh. "u' ak u' au pehkaya hunting na' etek etek'll sneak pa' tor wuh muskoka fau-yut. I losrak t'sai jane ne' tra'. I'll nem-tor du ha-kel. I suppose du've had hiyet t' ish-veh party." "ved, " leralmin-tor valancy meekly. Wuh wuh'rak ulef t' wuh yut ha-kel neither t' au leralmin-tor sovek-vel. Ish-veh would ri ma vesh' mau nam-tor-tor. T'sai jane tor ni mau ralash au kupi ri ma puzhu-tor tik vath. Anyway, valancy did ri olau conversationally vul-tor. She vesh' kafusik t' wuh bosh affairashamed t' ish-veh folly svi' goingashamed t' hasu afer-tor svi' such wuh shi k' barney snaith. K' barney snaith, reputed potau-tvi-shal-raf-shayek, infidel, forger heh defaulter. Valancy's bru-lar twitched svi' wuh mu'khlup'es u' she nahp t' ish-veh. Tonk'peh she vesh' kafusik. Heh wi she vesh' enjoying herselfwas bosh t' wuh flekh exultationbumping abru' ik rough fau-yut be' barney snaith. Wuh suk' lap pohshaya k' au. "ra wuh zan-tor hinek tom picked si' lu au torvau nash shack!" barney would leralmin exultantly. Mu'yor-yem vesh' wuh yem valancy tishau buhfik. Wuh faint laughter t' salan vesh' kwon-hau-ov pa' au heh wuh colours t' mistawis, imperial heh spiritual, ne' wuh rubai wan vesh' vel ik fam yehat nam-tor sagluvau svi' mere zhit. Duv, nuh'. Clustering svi' wuh pines abi' wuh salan hutau au si' heh pursued au abru' mistawis. Au ti ek' gad bi' wuh gef, threaded k' ferns heh kwai blossoms. Wuh aushfa, k' ish-veh kau-bosh, innocent pi' limuk, would hayal-tor fi' wuh verandah railing heh yokul wuh tidbits barney flung au. Heh uf rom kanok-vei zahv-tor! Valancy, svi' ek' wuh romance t' mistawis, worla forgot ik sasu had skaun-sa'haf. Barney vlitau ish-veh rai shaht t' compliments fi' ish-veh fasan. "po' ek', " au nafai-tor, "tra''s vel tor nam-tor leralmin-tor na' keh-vla yem. She had ri kauk wuh eku t' dishesonly barney's mismatched chipped bitsand wuh tal-kam, suk', pobby hinek mashek t' kushel's-yu-mur pla-kur. Po' wuh yem vesh' abru' au would hayal-tor tra' heh variben na' hoursor hayal-tor heh leralmin nothing, svi' ek' wuh gen-lis t' wuh panu, barney pulling maf na' ish-veh mev, valancy dreaming idly heh deliciously, gazing na' wuh irak-ska' kunel mesakh mistawis wilat wuh spires t' firs sasarlah tehnat wuh tev-tor. Wuh moonlight would palikau tor haul-tukh wuh mistawis dusk. Starok would palikau tor swoop darkly tehnat wuh spoh, western pi-maat-tukh. Wuh pi' waterfall ik sarlah ne' fi' wuh pid kutra ri irak maf would, k' ein whim t' wuh wildwood gods, palikau tor glazhau spo' wuh wonderful wan-kur kosu beckoning k'fai wuh spicy, svailik evergreens. Heh leander would palikau tor chuckle diabolically fi' wuh mainland gef. Uf slor ish-veh vesh' tor hayal-tor tra' heh tor nothing svi' wuh vaksurik silence, k' barney na' wuh vath vla t' wuh pasu, smoking! Tra' vesh' plenty t' vath vikuvtra svi' glan, hi rim vesh' be' hiyet tor nam-tor troublesome u' behsu. Tra' vesh' veh pi' travek t' islets irak ska' tor wuh tev'rak if au puvutau wuh fortunate isles. Na' ug'yel-shen au glazhau spo' wuh cluster t' yar-khush, na' tev-tor spo' wuh cluster t' gahv. Au vesh' nuh' pi' na' kelek; tonk'peh wuh ha'ge fi' wuh larger vikuvtra would svai si' ek' abru' wuh suk'muzh, heh bonfires would nam-tor lighted fi' ish-veh gef, streaming abru vi' wuh lapan duv heh throwing lo'uk, khaf-yon-kur ribbons abru' wuh mashau. Ralash-tanaf would maraya tor au alluringly s' masu-hali la' heh tra', il s' wuh verandahs fi' wuh suk' kelek t' wuh millionaire fi' wuh biggest vikuvtra. "would du spo' wuh kelek spo' ik, moonlight?" barney ya'akash wuh'wak, pral-tor ish-veh el'ru na' ish-veh. Au had taken tor calling ish-veh moonlight, heh valancy ashau ish-veh. "rai, " leralmin-tor valancy, vi had wuh'wak sahr-tor-tor t' wuh suk'kunel castle lehkuh wak wuh suk'es t' wuh don-ka sasu's "cottage" heh i' pitied wuh ri donku-tor inhabitants t' palaces. "rai. Ish-veh's nuh' sohkik. I would ma tor lesh ish-veh k' me kanok-wilat i went. Fi' t'nash-veh pla' spo' wuh snail. Ish-veh would sha' mepossess me, ak'shem heh soul. I ri tor envy hamilton gossard 'wuh finest belaar residence svi' canada.' ish-veh nam-tor magnificent, tonk'peh ish-veh isn't t'nash-veh pla-kur castle." maf ne' na' wuh irak shaht t' wuh suk'muzh au prah kanok mu-yor wuh glimpse t' wuh suk', continental ranau rushing k'fai wuh clearing. "ish-veh vesh' lovelybut i ri tor aitlun tor hal-tor va'ashiv, " leralmin-tor valancy. Ni wehk wadan wuh gad barney ikap-tor himself abru svi' bluebeard's tvi-shal. Valancy worla gla-tor wuh svi' ish-veh. S' wuh fnish-tor ik kapol-tor k'fai na' wak she concluded au bolau nam-tor conducting meli-tukh experimentsor counterfeiting donku. Valancy supposed tra' bolau nam-tor smelly patorau svi' tor counterfeit donku. Tonk'peh she did ri trouble herself pa' ish-veh. She had rai aitlun tor peer vi' wuh klacha tvi-shal t' barney's kelek t' ha'kiv. Ish-veh vesht heh ish-veh fa-wak concerned ish-veh ri. Goh nash rapturous la'. Nothing else mattered. Wuh'wak au went maf heh stayed maf dahkuh gad heh mu-yor. Au had ya'akash valancy kuv she would nam-tor kwes tor stay sa'awek heh she had leralmin-tor she would ri. Au worla var-tor ish-veh wilat au had vesh'. She vesh' ri kwes tor nam-tor sa'awek, tonk'peh she vesh' horribly lonely. Svi' pen, tor sovek duhsu vel du aitlu tor whenever wuh notion nem-tor du. Kuv ik wasn't el'es, ra vesh'? Chapter xxx au didn't spend ek' ish-veh gad fi' wuh vikuvtra.
