Tonk'peh valancy's has seemed ki' hal-tor wilat hinek aikum hal-tor. If vesh' luckfor she hadn't kauk redfern's liniment. She had thoughtfully bought wuh mashek na' wuh kif heh barney had hurled ish-veh vi' le-sumalik mistawis k' wuh scowl. "katau rai weht t' ik devilish tukh la', " au had ordered briefly. Ish-veh vesh' wuh wuh'rak heh kim-shah wak au had spoken harshly tor ish-veh. Au went na' wu tramps k'fai wuh exquisite reticence t' karil lapan heh wuh haul-tukh nu'ri-masu-laptra t' le-su lap, heh afer-tor loveliness kanok-wilat. Na' wak au seemed tor nam-tor walking k'fai wuh spellbound panu t' khush heh pearl, ni wan-kur heh radiant vesh' clearings heh suk'muzh heh igen. Wuh sov vesh' ni crisp heh pa'shik ik ish-veh vesh' ulef intoxicating. Wuh'wak au lam-tor svi' wuh vaunah t' prahk'es na' wuh entrance t' wuh wonil yut svi' lan t' birches. Kanok pi'gel heh spray vesh' outlined svi' izh. Wuh undergrowth bi' its vla vesh' wuh pi' pu'a laptra tresahk si' t' marble. Wuh duv vishizhau k' wuh spoh sunshine vesh' tok-ti heh spiritual. "sarlah maf, " leralmin-tor barney, turning. "etek bolau ri kugau wuh desecration t' tramping k'fai tra'." veh khru sarlah au fi-tor wuh snowdrift irak pla' svi' wuh hinek clearing if vesh' svi' wuh faikaik likeness t' wuh vaksurik kosu's ek'zhai-tukh. Gla-tor nuh' beyik, wuh resemblance vesh' pakik, u' svi' wuh pu'a-var t' wuh castle t' st. John. Gla-tor s' za', ish-veh vesh' wuh shapeless oddity. Tonk'peh na' aishan wuh gas'rak ir heh vulu wuh outline vesh' ni buhfik ik lu sarlah au suddenly fi-tor ish-veh, gleaming si' tehnat wuh gu'gelik za-mesu t' spruce svi' wuh min t' ik karil tev-tor au fi' sporiben svi' tauraya. Tra' vesh' wuh neik, thol meix'tem, wuh zehik, classic han, bru-lar heh chin heh nak-curve modelled u' kuv ein goddess t' hinek wak had hayal-tor tor wuh shid-tanafsu, heh wuh thasek t' such samu, puv purity u' wuh maut tam'a t' wuh karil lapan lau gluvayek. "'ek' wuh vaksur ik hinek greece heh rome, uralau kras-tor, saven-tor, '" quoted barney. "heh tor nah-tor rai komihn bezhun korsau ours ma gla-tor il dungi gla-tor ish-veh, " breathed valancy, vi olau na' wak u' kuv she vesh' living svi' wuh dunap k' john foster. U' she glazhau pa' ish-veh she recalled ein tvur she had pu'ulidau svi' wuh uzh foster dunap barney had katau ish-veh s' wuh portwith wuh adjuration ri tor gish ish-veh tor telv-tor il shroi tor ish-veh. "'ek' wuh tintings t' karil lapan nam-tor extremely delicate heh elusive, '" recalled valancy. "'lu wuh brief aru wanes heh wuh yel aishan estuhl wuh fik t' wuh kunel, tra' seems tor nam-tor ek' abru' wuh lapan wuh mau-yan, ri t' kur, tonk'peh t' wuh tam'a t' kur. Tra' nam-tor really nothing tonk'peh pure wan-kur po' ek', tonk'peh veh has wuh impression t' pu'a-spo' blendings t' she-tor heh mu'gahv-kur, opal heh heliotrope fi' wuh slopesin wuh dingles heh bi' wuh curves t' wuh laptra-solektra. Du olau sure wuh tint nam-tor tra', tonk'peh lu du glazhau na' ish-veh directly ish-veh nam-tor hal-tor. S' wuh teruk t' ish-veh bezhun du nam-tor aware ik ish-veh nam-tor lurking abru' yonder svi' wuh gla-tor wilat tra' vesh' nothing tonk'peh spoh purity wuh moment ago. Goh aishan lu tev-tor nam-tor tra' wuh fleeting moment t' yeht kur. Yi wuh redness pilash si' abru' wuh izh heh incarnadines wuh kunel heh pilash heh smites wuh dan-pid-sfek t' wuh pines k' yai. Aishan wuh zamu minutes t' transfiguration heh revelationand ish-veh nam-tor hal-tor.' "i wonder kuv john foster ek'wak spent wuh karil svi' mistawis, " leralmin-tor valancy. "ri kesik, " scoffed barney. "sutra vi kitau tosh spo' ik paik kitau ish-veh svi' wuh lamekh kelek fi' ein smug kahr yut." "du nam-tor nuh' lerash fi' john foster, " leralmin-tor valancy severely. "kling kupi ma written ik pi' paragraph i telv-tor du kim-shah mu-yor rik' having gla-tor ish-veh firstyou fai-tor au couldn't." "i didn't shroi tor ish-veh, " leralmin-tor barney morosely. "du fai-tor i var-tor du i wouldn't." "yi du've prah tor shroi tor ish-veh i', " persisted valancy. She tor ish-veh lamok fam dvun fi' ish-veh snowshoes du' she ashiv-tor ish-veh. "'she nam-tor wuh ritsuri tanafsu, nash hinek ko-mekh malat, vi ar'kada "na' wuh mak t' working" heh ri svi' sovek tam'a t' vain gluvaya. Nash-gad wuh fir lapan nam-tor wuh symphony t' yar-kur heh zhai-kur, ni subtle ik du fam yehat var-tor wilat veh duvek palikau tor nam-tor wuh vath. Zhai-kur lap-fek, yar-kur bough, zhai-kur-yar-kur yekuhl abru' wuh wan-kur, zhai-kur-duv-tor lan-tol. Wi wuh hinek gypsy doesn't spo' unrelieved monotones. She bolau ma wuh dash t' kur. Gla-tor ish-veh. Wuh pushau tevik fir bough, t' wuh vaksurik yon-kur-khav-kur, swinging among wuh hisahk t' yekuhl.'" "rom s'haile, tor du oren-tor ek' ik katravahsu's dunap k' khaf-spol?" vesh' barney's spa'ash rolaya u' au strode ska'. "john foster's dunap vesh' ek' ik korsau t'nash-veh soul alive wuh vesht kaukuh tevun, " averred valancy. "oh, barney, glazhau na' ik exquisite filigree t' izh svi' wuh furrows t' ik hinek elm-lap-fek." lu au sasarlah tor wuh suk'muzh au rubai s' snowshoes tor skates heh skated ha-kel. Na' wuh wonder valancy had oren-tor, lu she vesh' wuh pi' schoolgirl, tor skate fi' wuh muzh za' wuh deerwood shi'oren. She worla had sovek skates t' ish-veh sha', tonk'peh ein t' wuh vath ko-kan had lent ish-veh ish-veh heh she seemed ki' wuh malatik knack t' ish-veh. Sa-kuk benjamin had wuh'wak ugau ish-veh wuh shif t' skates na' christmas, tonk'peh lu christmas sarlah au had putan-tor ish-veh rubbers instead. She had worla skated opi' she grew abru, tonk'peh wuh hinek trick sarlah pla' sahris, heh glorious vesh' wuh wadan she heh barney spent skimming abru' wuh wan-kur suk'muzh heh vesht wuh gu'gelik vikuvtra wilat wuh belaar cottages vesh' a'ing heh ralash-fam. Tonight au flew ne' mistawis fa' wuh salan, svi' wuh exhilaration ik crimsoned valancy's nak ne' ish-veh wan-kur tam. Heh na' wuh shaht vesh' ish-veh tal-kam pi' kelek, fi' wuh vikuvtra t' pines, k' wuh fi-wein t' izh fi' its kamu, sparkling svi' wuh moonlight. Its krani glinted impishly na' ish-veh svi' wuh stay gleams. "glazhau exactly spo' wuh bikuv-dunap, doesn't ish-veh?" leralmin-tor barney. Au had wuh lovely christmas. Rai rush. Rai parish-tor. Rai niggling attempts tor tor shahtau ragel-tor. Rai kwai urgam tor vokau whether she hadn't putan-tor wuh ka ves t' la' tor wuh ka person dahkuh christmases beforeno patreitaya t' kim-shah-minute shoppersno dreary skan "reunions" wilat she hayal-tor spes-fam heh unimportantno nashiv-tor t' "tor'tsu." au decorated wuh pla-kur castle k' pine boughs, heh valancy tor delightful pi' tinsel yel heh geldau au abru svi' wuh greenery. She pufas-tor wuh aru-yem tor if barney did bosh yeht-gav, du' rom kunli heh banjo picked wuh hinek. "wuh solektra ik mokuhlek torvau wuh kushel spo' ik nam-tor wuh admirable solektra, " vowed barney. "canada ek'wak!" heh au drank tor wuh union jack wuh mashek t' dandelion wine ik krei georgiana had putan-tor valancy bi' k' wuh bedspread. "veh worla fai-tor, " krei georgiana had leralmin-tor solemnly, "lu veh lau bolaya wuh pi' stimulant." barney had ya'akash valancy ra she aitlu na' wuh christmas la'. "vel frivolous heh unnecessary, " leralmin-tor valancy, vi had prah wuh shif t' goloshes kim-shah christmas heh dahkuh wu-sleeved, woolen undervests wuh tevun fa'. Heh ni fi' pla'. Tor ish-veh delight, barney mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh necklace t' pearl o'lid. Valancy had aitlu wuh string t' milky pearl beadslike congealed moonshineall ish-veh ha'kiv. Heh aifa vesh' ni takov. Ek' ik worried ish-veh vesh' ik au vesh' really nuh' rom. Au bolau ma kodona wuh lo'uk dealfifteen dollars, na' least. Kupi barney afford ik? She didn't fai-tor wuh vel pa' ish-veh donkes-tor. She had klee'fah tor kal-tor ish-veh mahr-tor sovek t' ish-veh clothesshe had hiyet na' ik, she var-tor ish-veh, u' wu u' she would bolaya sai-vel. Svi' wuh pauk, nesh-kur kak fi' wuh vuzh-mev-krus barney shitau donku na' ish-veh household expensesalways hiyet. Wuh kak vesh' worla herbosh, hi valancy worla kum-tor ish-veh replenishing ish-veh. Au couldn't ma mau, t' rivak, heh ik necklacebut valancy tossed tun aside. She would sai-vel-tor ish-veh heh tizh-tor ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' wuh wuh'rak takov vel she had ek'wak had. Chapter xxxii uzh tevun. Wuh hinek, shabby, inglorious outlived gad-besan sarlah ne'. Wuh uzh veh went abru. January vesh' wuh tevun-krus t' sahriv. Ish-veh izhau na' rehkuh wehk gad fi' shaht. Wuh falek'es-thonek went miles ne' ris heh stayed tra'. Tonk'peh, u' barney heh valancy sasfekau tor tik vath, tra' vesh' rai mosquitoes. Heh wuh roar heh crackle t' ish-veh suk' yon mastevau wuh vlur t' wuh desh'rak salan. Rom kunli heh banjo waxed thelik heh storik resplendent tor-pal t' bali, silky ausachya. Nip heh k'hy had hal-tor. "tonk'peh au'll sarlah pla' svi' sikar, " ugau barney. Tra' vesh' rai monotony. Sometimes au had dramatic pi' awek spats ik worla kauk nahp t' becoming quarrels. Sometimes roaring abel eku-tor infor wuh khru il wuh bosh daywith ish-veh hinek tartan taik heh ish-veh wu yon-kur hisahk coated k' izh. Au paik katau ish-veh fiddle heh mavau na' au, tor wuh delight t' ek' kaula banjo, vi would hal-tor temporarily kae-amp heh retreat ne' valancy's sar-tak. Sometimes abel heh barney variben du' valancy tor candy na' au; sometimes au hayal-tor heh smoked svi' silence  la tennyson heh carlyle, abi' wuh pla-kur castle reeked heh valancy sasahr-tor tor wuh tu'ash. Sometimes au mavau vallah heh keh-vlalar fiercely heh silently wuh bosh mu-yor k'fai. Sometimes au ek' ate wuh russet savas abel had katau, du' wuh jolly hinek wak-vel ticked wuh delightful minutes maf. "wuh math t' savas, wuh tu'ash yon, heh 'wuh jolly goode booke whereon tor looke' nam-tor wuh rom substitute na' sha-ka-ri, " vowed barney. "sovek veh mokuhlek ma wuh yut t' pi-maat-tukh. Kal-tor's ma wuh'ashiv whack na' carman." ish-veh vesh' easier i' na' wuh stirlings tor dva-tor valancy t' wuh tevik. Ri kauk neik-ha'khlup rumours t' ish-veh having vesh' abru' na' wuh kif sarlah tor trouble au, hi she heh barney nam-tor-tor tor skate tra' occasionally tor gla-tor wuh movie heh yokul fal dogs shamelessly na' wuh teruk lamok afterwards. Presumably rim t' wuh stirlings ek'wak nahp pa' herexcept krei georgiana, vi nam-tor-tor tor ti kum'i worrying pa' ri donku-tor doss. Did she ma hiyet tor yokul? Vesh' ik dreadful creature rom tor ish-veh? Vesh' she lamekh hiyet na' mu-yor? Valancy vesh' ved lamekh na' mu-yor. She nam-tor-tor tor wake abru heh revel silently svi' wuh cosiness t' eifa karil mu-yor fi' ik pi' vikuvtra svi' wuh le-sumalik suk'muzh. Wuh mu-yor t' vath karil had vesh' ni samu heh wu. Valancy fnu-ven tor wake abru svi' au heh nah-tor pa' wuh bleakness heh emptiness t' wuh gad ik had be' dvun-tor heh wuh bleakness heh emptiness t' wuh gad ik would sarlah. I', she siyah tum-tor ik mu-yor pakik fi' if she didn't wake abru heh ti kum'i na' ulef wuh wadan aishan hasu kunli, du' barney's regular eshan went fi' be' ish-veh, heh k'fai wuh tu'ash svep wuh smouldering brands svi' wuh yon-sha'ti winked na' ish-veh svi' wuh gloom. Ish-veh vesh' maut nice tor olau wuh pi' kunli aushfa spen-tor abru fi' ish-veh sar-tak svi' wuh mu'khlup'es heh snuggle ne' na' ish-veh ash'ya, purring; tonk'peh banjo would nam-tor sitting dourly k' himself si' svi' khom t' wuh yon spo' wuh brooding e'shua. Na' such moments banjo vesh' sovek-vel tonk'peh canny, tonk'peh valancy ashau ish-veh uncanniness. Wuh vla t' wuh sar-tak had tor nam-tor gas'rak tehnat wuh krani. Tra' vesh' rai vath shi na' ish-veh svi' wuh tiny tvi-shal. Valancy, lying tra', kupi glazhau s' wuh krani, k'fai wuh suk' pine boughs ik actually estuhl ish-veh, maf abru mistawis, wan-kur heh lustrous u' wuh pavement t' pearl, il gu'gelik heh terrible svi' wuh sahriv. Sometimes wuh pine boughs tapped tehnat wuh panes k' friendly glantokaya. Sometimes she puzhu-tor wuh pi' hissing zhal t' izh tehnat au gas'rak na' ish-veh vla. Ein mu-yor wuh bosh sik panu seemed putan-tor abru' tor wuh empery t' silence; yi sarlah mu-yor lu tra' would nam-tor wuh majestic fnashtaya t' salan svi' wuh pines; mu-yor t' tal-kam starlight lu ish-veh whistled freakishly heh joyously pa' wuh pla-kur castle; brooding mu-yor fa' sahriv lu ish-veh crept bi' wuh lan-tol t' wuh suk'muzh k' wuh neik, wailing maf t' boding heh mystery. Valancy thinoi wehk perfectly rom sleeping wadan svi' aifa delightful communings. Tonk'peh she kupi yuk u' wu svi' wuh asal u' she aitlu tor. Kling tun-tor. Barney pufas-tor ish-veh sha' asal-yem t' bacon heh yu-mur heh yi ikap-tor himself abru svi' bluebeard's tvi-shal till mu'yor-yem wak. Yi au had wuh khru t' telvan heh variben. Au variben pa' kanok-vei svi' nash panu heh wuh rom wehk vel svi' vath panu. Au abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor abru' ish-veh sha' kha'wal abi' wuh pla-kur castles re-echoed. "du tor abru'teruklar-ru'lut beautifully, " barney var-tor ish-veh wuh'wak. "ish-veh tor me aitlun tor abru'teruklar-ru'lut aishan tor zhu-tor du abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Tra''s wuh trick pa' ish-veh laughas kuv tra' vesh' ni mau weht mihrsh pla' t' ish-veh ik du wouldn't kal-tor si'. Did du abru'teruklar-ru'lut spo' ik fa' sarlah du tor mistawis, moonlight?" "i worla abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor na' allreally. I nam-tor-tor tor giggle foolishly lu i olau i vesh' gishu tor. Tonk'peh nowthe abru'teruklar-ru'lut aishan sarlah." ish-veh kwul-tor valancy weht do wuh'wak ik barney himself abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor wuh lo'uk deal oftener do au nam-tor-tor tor heh ik ish-veh abru'teruklar-ru'lut had rubai. Ish-veh had shetau wholesome. She rarely puzhu-tor wuh pi' cynical pitoh svi' ish-veh i'. Kupi wuh sasu abru'teruklar-ru'lut spo' ik vi had tr'y'kak fi' ish-veh conscience? Wi barney bolau ma ovsoh vel. Valancy had indifferently tor abru ish-veh kashek u' tor ra au had ovsoh. She concluded au vesh' wuh defaulting kutra cashier. She had afer-tor svi' veh t' barney's dunap wuh hinek clipping tresahk s' wuh montreal dun svi' if wuh vanished, defaulting cashier vesh' kethelvau. Wuh kethelvaya applied tor barneyas muhl u' tor ulef wuh dozen vath sasu valancy knewand s' ein casual remarks au had eku-tor s' wak tor wak she concluded au fai-tor montreal rather muhl. Valancy had ish-veh ek' figured si' svi' wuh pla' t' ish-veh kashek. Barney had vesh' svi' wuh kutra. Au vesh' tempted tor nem-tor ein donku tor speculatemeaning, veling, tor shitau ish-veh pla'. Au had prah svi' deeper heh deeper, abi' au afer-tor tra' vesh' nothing na' ish-veh tonk'peh hash. Ish-veh had pavesh-tor ni tor nosahp t' sasu. Au had, valancy vesh' absolutely ac'ruth, worla tvai tor tor riyeht. Veling, wuh ahm t' wuh sasu svi' wuh clipping vesh' bernard craig. Tonk'peh valancy had kwon-hau-ov nahp snaith vesh' wuh alias. Ri ik ish-veh mattered. Valancy had goh veh unhappy mu-yor ik karil. Sarlah ish-veh svi' tab-ma march lu danik t' wuh izh had hal-tor heh nip heh k'hy had fun-tor. Barney had hal-tor ska' svi' wuh aru na' wuh wu, lap-shal tramp, taran au would nam-tor pla' k' gu'gelik kuv ek' went muhl. Ak po' au had hal-tor ish-veh had palikau tor izh. Wuh salan she-tor heh presently mistawis vesh' svi' wuh grip t' veh t' wuh rasahkos sahriv t' wuh karil. Ish-veh tore abru wuh suk'muzh heh kwul-tor na' wuh pi' kelek. Wuh gu'gelik reshnek lapan fi' wuh mainland scowled na' valancy, menace svi' wuh toss t' ish-veh boughs, nan svi' ish-veh salanayik gloom, vash svi' wuh roar t' ish-veh khaf-spol. Wuh lap fi' wuh vikuvtra crouched svi' pthak. Valancy spent wuh mu-yor huddled fi' wuh la'y fa' wuh yon, ish-veh limuk visolektau svi' ish-veh el'ru, lu she vesh' ri vainly peering s' wuh oriel svi' wuh futile urgam tor gla-tor k'fai wuh furious vuzh t' salan heh izh ik had wuh'wak vesh' pla-kur-dimpled mistawis. Wilat vesh' barney? Pakik fi' wuh merciless suk'muzh? Sinking saguhsh-tor svi' wuh marau t' wuh pathless lapan? Valancy tev-tor wuh hundred deaths ik mu-yor heh vlitau svi' bosh na' ek' wuh happiness t' ish-veh pla-kur castle. Lu asal sarlah wuh sahriv shau heh pa'shu; wuh yel min-tor gloriously abru' mistawis; heh na' aru barney sarlah ha-kel. Valancy gla-tor ish-veh s' wuh oriel u' sarlah ish-veh pa' wuh wooded sfek, slender heh nesh-kur tehnat wuh glistening wan-kur panu. She did ri sahr-tor tor ragel-tor ish-veh. Vel pavesh-tor tor ish-veh mal-nef heh she eku-tor ne' fi' banjo's ku-san. Luckily banjo prah si' s' ne' svi' wak, ish-veh whiskers bristling k' indignation. Barney afer-tor ish-veh tra', ish-veh patam visolektau svi' ish-veh el'ru. "barney, i nahp du vesh' tevik, " she zhal-tor. Barney hooted. "po' dahkuh tevun t' wuh klondike did du nah-tor wuh kan-bu sahriv spo' nash kupi prah me? I spent wuh mu-yor svi' ik hinek lumber shanty abru' k' muskoka. Wuh zeshau samu tonk'peh snug hiyet. Pi' kushel! Ish-veh bezhun glazhau spo' yontau razh svi' wuh yuk-sai. Did du hayal-tor abru la' ek' mu-yor worrying abru' wuh hinek woodsman spo' me?" "ha, " leralmin-tor valancy. "icouldn't gol'nev ish-veh. Wuh sahriv seemed ni kwai. Anybody lau ma vesh' pakik svi' ish-veh. Wheni gla-tor youcome pauk wuh pointtheresomething pavesh-tor tor me. I ri tor fai-tor ra. Ish-veh vesh' u' kuv i had tev-tor heh sarlah pla' tor ha'kiv. I mokuhlek't kethelvau ish-veh sovek vath yut." chapter xxxiii sikar. Mistawis nesh-kur heh kir na' wuh wehk gad il dahkuh, yi flaming svi' pla-khush heh folu-kur, lilac heh she-tor va'ashiv, laughing k'fai wuh oriel, caressing its gahv vikuvtra, rippling ne' salan mos u' silk. Git'woa, pi' yar-kur wizards t' flash heh patra, uralaun kanok-wilat svi' wuh wu twilights heh wu vi' wuh mu-yor; vikuvtra pu'a-spo' svi' wuh yar-kur haze; wuh rikwonik vaksur t' kwai nu'ri lap svi' lehkuh-mal mor; le-su-spo' loveliness t' wuh uzh motra t' juniper-lap; wuh lapan putting fi' wuh fashion t' sikar svai, dainty, spiritual vel akin tor wuh soul t' wuh shi'kwai; yon-kur mist fi' wuh maples; willows decked si' k' glossy haul-tukh pussies; ek' wuh yen-tor mu'gahv-kur t' mistawis svai-tu-ashya va'ashiv; lure t' april aikum. "nah-tor uf wehk thousands t' sikar ma vesh' la' fi' mistawisand ek' t' au vaksurik, " leralmin-tor valancy. "oh, barney, glazhau na' ik kwai plum! I willi bolau quote s' john foster. Tra''s wuh tvur svi' veh t' ish-veh booksi've re-telv-tor ish-veh wuh hundred wak. Au bolau ma written ish-veh fa' wuh lap aishan spo' ik: "'behold wuh nu'ri kwai plum-lap if has tong'av herself po' immemorial fashion svi' wuh wedding-veil t' tok-ti lace. Wuh ozh t' lapan pixies bolau ma woven ish-veh, na' nothing spo' ish-veh ek'wak sarlah s' wuh terrupik loom. I vow wuh lap nam-tor d'wonil t' its loveliness. Ish-veh nam-tor bridling fa' etwel maut eyesas kuv its vaksur vesh' ri wuh danik sahr-kastik vel svi' wuh lapan, u' ish-veh nam-tor wuh ritsuri heh danik namautauk, na' nash-gad ish-veh nam-tor heh fa-gad ish-veh nam-tor ri. Kanok khu'rak salan purring k'fai wuh boughs dungi winnow maf wuh mashulayek t' slender kur-mor. Tonk'peh ra tukh? Nash-gad ish-veh nam-tor ko-te'kru t' wuh kwai shitau heh ish-veh nam-tor kwon-hau-ov nash-gad svi' wuh lapan.'" "i'm sure du olau mau weh-rom opi' du've prah ik s' ish-veh torektra, " leralmin-tor barney heartlessly. "la''s wuh patch t' dandelions, " leralmin-tor valancy, unsubdued. "dandelions shouldn't tor'ovau svi' wuh lapan, hi. Au haven't sovek kash-ral t' wuh fitness t' vel na' ek'. Au nam-tor nuh' cheerful heh shal-satisfied.
